Z chosen for zero-JS sync, broad browser support, and natural future extension to a 3-pane layout when a resource panel lands.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 4.5)

- **`position: sticky` requires a scrollport ancestor.** The header SVG sticks relative to the nearest scroll container (the wrapper div with `overflow: auto`). If the wrapper's overflow stays `visible` (the default), sticky promotes to a more distant scroll container (e.g. `body` or `.cx-demo-svg-frame`), which collapses the intended pinning. Library inlines `overflow: auto` on the wrapper to guarantee a scrollport without requiring consumers to set it.
- **Sticky has no visible effect when the scrollport never actually scrolls.** With `overflow: auto` but no height cap, the wrapper grows to fit content and no scroll engages — sticky degrades to `position: static` semantically (header still flows in normal position). The consumer's CSS controls when sticky activates (e.g. demo sets `.cx-gantt-wrapper { max-height: 70vh }`). Document this in the wrapper's inline comment so a future maintainer doesn't add height to the library default.
- **`width: max-content` for screenshot capture, NOT for production.** The wrapper's `display: block` default makes its bounding box clamp to the parent's content-area width (= viewport width). A wider-than-viewport body SVG paints past the wrapper's box, but `locator.screenshot()` captures only the bbox — so a year-view (~24000 px) capture would miss everything past viewport-width. Solution: the VRT spec's hide-chrome CSS adds `width: max-content !important` on the wrapper so its bbox hugs the natural content width. The library does NOT ship `width: max-content`; the production wrapper stays block-sized so consumers can lay it out with regular CSS techniques.
- **Header SVG must occlude the body during scroll.** With `position: sticky; top: 0` the header floats over the body as the user scrolls vertically — without an opaque `background` on the header, bars peek through. Inline `background: #ffffff; z-index: 1` settles this. `z-index: 1` only matters in the (rare) case the body SVG is itself positioned and would otherwise stack equal-or-above the header.
- **happy-dom's `getBoundingClientRect()` returns `{0, 0, 0, 0}` for un-laid-out SVGs.** Test code reads pointer coords as `e.clientX - rect.left` → `e.clientX - 0` → `clientX`. With the old single-SVG root, the test had to add `headerBandHeight (44)` to clientY to land inside the bar area (because content-y 0 was 44 below SVG top). After splitting into separate SVGs, the body SVG's origin IS content-y 0 — `cy = 20` directly hits row 1. Updated ~30 SFC tests to drop the `+ 44` offset.
- **Vue's `style` prop accepts objects; `zIndex` camelCase auto-serializes to `z-index`.** Used inline-style objects throughout (`style: { position: 'sticky', top: '0', zIndex: 1, background: '#ffffff' }`) for clarity. The serialized DOM gets `style="position: sticky; top: 0px; z-index: 1; background: rgb(255, 255, 255);"` — happy-dom's CSSOM accepts `el.style.position === 'sticky'` for assertions.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 4.5)

- **Commit 1** (`01f2cfe`) — structural refactor. `<ChronixGantt>` returns a `<div class="cx-gantt-wrapper">` containing two SVG children: `<svg class="cx-gantt-header">` (header rows + tick row) on top of `<svg class="cx-gantt-body">` (bar group, no translate — body SVG's origin IS content-y 0). Pointer handlers move to the body SVG only; the header SVG has no listeners (axis-row clicks silently no-op). `toContentXY` reads from the body SVG's bbox and drops the `headerBandHeight` subtraction. The `if (pos.y < 0) return` filter becomes a safety net. ~30 SFC tests updated: `wrapper.find('svg')` → `wrapper.find('svg.cx-gantt-body')`, clientY values dropped by 44 (default band) or 70 (custom band) to compensate. The two old "header-band-filter" tests collapse into one safety-net test that fires `pointerdown` with negative clientY directly on the body SVG.
- **Commit 2** (`070841c`) — sticky positioning. Wrapper div gets inline `overflow: auto`; header SVG gets inline `position: sticky; top: 0; z-index: 1; background: #ffffff; display: block`; body SVG gets inline `display: block`. Demo's `.cx-demo-svg-frame` drops `overflow: auto + max-height: 70vh` (scroll moves one level inward); demo's `.cx-gantt-wrapper { max-height: 70vh }` constrains the wrapper height so sticky actually engages. Three new SFC tests assert the inline contract (overflow on wrapper, sticky+top+background on header, header.width === body.width). 80 → 83 vue3 tests.
- **Commit 3** (`65be661`) — VRT rebaseline. `chronix-visual.spec.ts` targets `div.cx-gantt-wrapper` (was `svg.cx-gantt`); hide-chrome CSS adds `width: max-content !important` on the wrapper + the demo frame so the wrapper's bbox hugs natural content width. The 5 recaptured PNGs are byte-for-byte near-identical to the pre-refactor baselines (5-byte zlib delta per file, well under `maxDiffPixelRatio: 0.001`) — empirical evidence the split-SVG render is pixel-equivalent to the old single-SVG render.
- **Browser-side verification (out-of-band).** Wrote `D:/tmp/sticky-verify/verify-sticky.mjs` to drive both demos (k-ui at 8701, chronix at 8702) and capture full-natural-width screenshots per view. Confirmed visually: chronix's sticky header pins to wrapper top during vertical scroll, horizontal scroll moves header + body in lockstep (shared parent scroll, no JS sync handler).

### Naming justifications (Phase 4.5)

- **`cx-gantt-wrapper` / `cx-gantt-header` / `cx-gantt-body`** (vs reusing `cx-gantt`): the old single-class was an SVG marker. The wrapper is now a structural container, not the SVG itself. Each child has its own role-tagged class so consumers can style or test them independently. Dropping `cx-gantt` from the wrapper avoids the confusing situation where `wrapper.find('svg.cx-gantt')` returns nothing despite the wrapper still being "the chart" — explicit names make the test queries grep-clear.
- **`bodySvgRef`** (vs reusing `svgRef`): the ref now points to the body SVG specifically. Renaming makes pointer-math reading obvious: anywhere the code reads `bodySvgRef.value.getBoundingClientRect()`, it's reading the body's geometry, not "the SVG's" (ambiguous now that there are two).

### Open / parked (Phase 4.5)

- **Resource panel still missing.** The reference demo's full layout is 3-pane (sidebar columns + header + body). chronix's wrapper is 2-pane (header + body). When the resource panel lands, Z extends naturally: a `display: grid` wrapper with sidebar column on the left (sticky-left), header row on top-right (sticky-top), body bottom-right. No JS scroll-sync needed at any pane boundary — CSS sticky handles both axes. Park behind a dedicated phase.
- **`max-height` is consumer-controlled.** With no cap, the wrapper grows unboundedly. Library doesn't ship a default cap because "how tall should a gantt be?" is application-specific. The example app caps at `70vh` to make the sticky behavior demonstrable. A future docs page should document this expectation.
- **Header inline-style vs CSS-class.** The header SVG ships with `position: sticky; …; background: #ffffff` as inline style. A consumer who wants dark theme has to override via `!important` or by writing inline style themselves. A future tokenized-theme phase could expose `--cx-gantt-header-bg`. Park.
- **Sticky-pinning has no automated VRT test.** A sticky-header screenshot would require driving a scroll mid-test and capturing twice (before / after). The SFC tests cover the inline-style contract; a future Phase 3.dd "interaction-recording goldens" (parked in Phase 4.4) could add the visual sticky-scroll test.
- **k-ui side VRT baselines still incomplete for wider views.** Out of scope for Phase 4.5 — chronix-side rebaseline is the priority.

## Phase 4.5 — DONE

- 3 commits: `01f2cfe` (structural refactor) + `070841c` (sticky positioning) + `65be661` (VRT rebaseline). Net: `<ChronixGantt>` root is now `<div class="cx-gantt-wrapper" style="overflow: auto">` containing `<svg class="cx-gantt-header" style="position: sticky; top: 0; z-index: 1; background: #ffffff; display: block">` and `<svg class="cx-gantt-body" style="display: block">`. Demo's `.cx-gantt-wrapper { max-height: 70vh }` engages the sticky scroll.
- 83 vue3-adapter tests (was 80; +3 sticky-contract assertions). 178 core gantt tests unchanged. Total cumulative vitest 261. 22 parity assertions unchanged.
- 5 chronix VRT baselines re-captured at natural content width (1440 / 2015 / 5980 / 11960 / 23725 px). PNGs are byte-near-identical to pre-refactor (within `maxDiffPixelRatio: 0.001`).
- ci-check fully green. Browser-verified: sticky header pins during vertical scroll, header+body move in lockstep horizontally.

## Phase 5 — ResourceArea sidebar (2026-05-15)

### Reference reading (Phase 5)

- `packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceList.tsx` (573 lines) — the reference's resource-panel implementation. Table-based DOM (`<table class="gantt-resource-list">` with `<colgroup>` + `<thead>` + `<tbody>`), `rowSpan` cells for hierarchical grouping (parent values merged across N consecutive child rows), inline-SVG expander glyph, depth-based indent on the main column, `ContentContainer` wrappers around every cell to support custom-content callbacks + lifecycle hooks. `ResourceColumnSpec.isMain` flag distinguishes the "Resources" column (gets indented expander) from auxiliary columns. State: `expandedGroups: Set<string>` toggled by clicking a group row.
- `packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineLayout.tsx` (header.left wiring at line 249) — confirms the left header is a sibling table with the same column widths, height matched to the chart header band via measured layout.
- The chronix `RowSpec.columns: Readonly<Record<string, string | number | undefined>>` field (defined since Phase 1) — already in the public IR. Demo's `sampleRows` populates `{ name: '车间 A' }` etc. The sidebar's job is to render this map column-by-column.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 5)

- **`position: sticky` in two dimensions is a one-property generalization of Phase 4.5's sticky-top.** With the wrapper as the scrollport, `sticky; top: 0; left: 0` on the top-left corner element pins it under any combination of horizontal + vertical scroll. The browser's compositor solves the sync; no JS handler is needed. The reference's JS scroll-sync between four panes (header-right ⇄ body-right, body-left ⇄ body-right) is a pre-`position:sticky` workaround.
- **CSS grid with `grid-template-columns: ${sidebarWidth}px auto` makes the wrapper a 2-track container that grows to fit the chart.** The `auto` track sizes to its content's intrinsic width (`max-content` of the body SVG = the chart's natural pixel width). The grid's overall intrinsic width = sidebarWidth + chart natural width. The wrapper's existing `overflow: auto` then engages horizontal scroll exactly as it did pre-sidebar. Using `1fr` instead of `auto` would fail: `1fr` resolves to "available space" so the grid's width never exceeds the wrapper's own width, no horizontal overflow detected, no scroll.
- **Z-index ladder ensures correct paint stacking at corner intersections.** When both axes scroll, the four panes geometrically overlap at the corners: top-left corner of every pane lands on top of the corner just before it. Without z-index, the body SVG (last in source order) would paint OVER the sidebar-body at the left-edge crossing and OVER the chart-header at the top-edge crossing. Monotone ladder (`sidebar-header: 3 > chart-header: 2 > sidebar-body: 1 > body: auto`) makes the correct pane win at each crossing. The opaque `background: #ffffff` on each non-default pane ensures the painting actually occludes (transparency would defeat the ladder).
- **`width: max-content` on a `display: grid` container resolves to the sum of intrinsic track widths.** For the VRT capture (which needs the wrapper's bbox to hug natural content for full-width screenshots), `width: max-content !important` on the grid wrapper produces `sidebarWidth + max-content of chart` — exactly the same result the natural overflow would produce, just promoted to the wrapper's own bbox.
- **happy-dom serializes Vue inline style objects predictably.** `style: { position: 'sticky', top: '0', left: '0', zIndex: 3 }` → `el.style.position === 'sticky'`, `el.style.top === '0px'`, `el.style.left === '0px'`, `el.style.zIndex === '3'`. The `zIndex` camelCase auto-serializes to `z-index` CSS property; the value is stringified ("3" not 3). Tests read via `Number(el.style.zIndex)` to compare numerically.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 5)

- **Pre-implementation catalog** (commit `8d14377`) — extended `audit/PHASE_5_RESOURCE_AREA_DESIGN.md` with a 27-item k-ui resource-panel behavior surface, each tagged ✅ done / ⏸️ parked / ❌ rejected. Three cohesive parking groups identified (tree-grouping; custom renderers; theming + resize). The catalog exists to defend against drift: silently dropping a sub-behavior is the failure mode of an R2 rewrite.
- **Commit 1** (`d378b3d`) — structural. Added `ColumnSpec` interface (exported from `@chronixjs/gantt-vue3`) and optional `columns?: ColumnSpec[]` prop on `<ChronixGantt>`. When non-empty, the wrapper switches to `display: grid; grid-template-columns: ${sidebarWidth}px auto`; sidebar-header (top-left) renders column labels in a sub-grid, sidebar-body (bottom-left) renders one row per swimlane strip with each row's cells reading `RowSpec.columns[col.key]`. When omitted or empty `[]`, the DOM is unchanged from Phase 4.5 — zero cost for existing consumers. 11 new SFC tests (83 → 94).
- **Commit 2** (`8d9648a`) — sticky positioning. Inline `position: sticky; top: 0; left: 0; z-index: 3` on sidebar-header; `position: sticky; left: 0; z-index: 1` on sidebar-body; chart-header's z-index bumped from `1` to `2` so it slots between the sidebar panes. Opaque `background: #ffffff` on both new panes preserves the occlusion contract. 3 new SFC contract tests (94 → 97).
- **Commit 3** (`45403f3`) — demo wiring + VRT rebaseline. Example app passes `columns="[{ key: 'name', label: '车间', width: 120 }]"`. The sample rows already had `{ name: '车间 A' }` etc. — single-column sidebar is the natural minimal demo. 5 chronix VRT PNGs re-captured; each grew by exactly 120 px in width (the sidebar), heights unchanged.

### Naming justifications (Phase 5)

- **`ColumnSpec`** (vs `ResourceColumnSpec` from the reference): the type lives in `@chronixjs/gantt-vue3`'s exports, where the context already implies "for the gantt's resource panel". The redundant `Resource` prefix would crowd the public surface. Reference uses `ResourceColumnSpec` because their core has multiple non-resource column types (event-column, calendar-column variants); chronix has just one.
- **`columns`** (prop name, vs `resourceColumns` or `colSpecs`): matches the conventional CSS-table parlance (`<colgroup>` / `<col>`) and the existing `RowSpec.columns` field they read from. Naming symmetry: `rows: RowSpec[]` + `columns: ColumnSpec[]`.
- **`cx-gantt-sidebar-{header,body,row,cell,header-cell}`** (class names, vs `cx-gantt-resource-{...}`): "sidebar" describes the geometric pane (left-anchored, sticky-left); "resource" is the application-domain concept that the pane displays. Pane name lives at the DOM layer (closer to CSS); domain name lives at the data layer (closer to consumer code). `RowSpec`/`ColumnSpec` already carry the domain semantics.
- **`data-row-id`** (mirrors `RowSpec.id`, vs k-ui's `data-resource-id`): chronix-native naming, `RowSpec` is the IR identifier.

### Open / parked (Phase 5)

- **Tree-grouping** (rowSpan merge cells + expand/collapse + depth-indent + group rows + sticky cushion + state CSS classes + inline expander glyph) — parked as one cohesive future phase. All items depend on a tree pre-pass that walks adjacent rows by shared column values to emit `rowSpan` counts. Demo currently uses flat rows so no user-visible behavior gap.
- **Custom renderers** (`ColumnSpec.cellContent` callback, `headerContent`, `isMain` flag with `"Resources"` fallback, `RowSpec.title` + `getPublicId` fallback, component-level `resourceLabelContent` prop) — parked as one cohesive future phase. v0 hardcodes `String(row.columns[key])` and `String(col.label)`.
- **Theme tokens** — `background` is currently hardcoded `#ffffff` inline. Future phase exposes `--cx-gantt-sidebar-bg` / `--cx-gantt-header-bg` etc. CSS variables.
- **Resizable column widths** — k-ui supports drag-resize of column dividers; chronix v0 takes fixed `ColumnSpec.width` pixels. Drag-resize lives outside `ResourceList.tsx` in the reference; needs separate audit.
- **Auto-width columns** rejected — consumers compute widths and pass them; keeps VRT deterministic.
- **`data-row-index` attribute** rejected — render-order-dependent identifier is fragile across row reorderings; consumers should query by `data-row-id`.
- **k-ui resource-panel "right column" parity** (e.g. monthly summary columns at the right edge of the resource panel) — not in scope; reference's vue3 demo doesn't exercise this.

## Phase 5 — DONE

- 4 commits: `8d14377` (k-ui behavior catalog) + `d378b3d` (structural) + `8d9648a` (sticky + z-index) + `45403f3` (demo wiring + VRT rebaseline). `<ChronixGantt>` accepts optional `columns: ColumnSpec[]` prop; when set, the wrapper is a 2×2 CSS grid with sticky-left sidebar panes; when omitted, DOM is unchanged from Phase 4.5.
- 97 vue3-adapter tests (was 83; +11 sidebar contract + +3 sticky contract). 178 core gantt tests unchanged. **Total cumulative vitest 275.** 22 parity assertions unchanged.
