## Phase 20.7 — Cross-demo screenshot diff infrastructure (DONE, 2026-05-16)

Third infrastructure phase of the 2026-05-16 session. Adds a pixel-level
visual regression layer that complements the DOM-level parity layer
landed in Phase 20.5. Two complementary registries share one capture
pipeline: 12 `kind: 'cross'` scenarios diff chronix vs k-ui pixel-by-pixel,
13 `kind: 'vrt'` scenarios diff chronix against its own frozen baseline
(for chronix-only toggles where k-ui has no analog). Fixed tolerance
across all 25: `maxDiffPixelRatio: 0` + `threshold: 0.2` — "pixel-perfect
modulo AA". `/phase-close` gains a new step 6.5 that runs
`pnpm cross-demo-verify` before any future phase can flip Status to DONE.

### Reference reading (Phase 20.7)

- `D:/work/chronix/tooling/golden-runner/playwright.config.ts` — existing snapshot infrastructure (`snapshotDir: ./goldens`, `snapshotPathTemplate: {snapshotDir}/{arg}{ext}`). Phase 20.7 lands baselines under `goldens/cross-demo-baselines/{kui,chronix}/<id>.png` — separate subdir keeps cross-demo distinct from the existing 5 chronix VRT + 6 k-ui parity goldens at the root.
- `D:/work/chronix/tooling/golden-runner/tests/chronix-visual.spec.ts` — the existing CSS-injection pattern that hides chronix's demo chrome before screenshotting. Phase 20.7 factors this into a shared `hidePageChrome(page, source)` private helper inside `parity-helpers.ts`, source-specific.
- `D:/work/chronix/tooling/golden-runner/src/reference-dom-map.ts` — the allow-listed boundary for k-ui-side CSS class names. Phase 20.7's `hidePageChrome('kui', ...)` interpolates `TIMELINE_BODY_WRAPPER` from this map (vs inlining the literal `.gantt-timeline-body-wrapper`), preserving the no-external-repo-refs invariant.
- `D:/work/chronix/examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue` (post-Phase-20.6) — confirms chronix's URL-config layer exposes `parity` / `priorityCallback` / `themedBars` / `umbrellaColor` / `editable` / `selectable` / 4 Phase 19 validator toggles. The 25-scenario registry's `urlQuery` field encodes combinations of these.
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` — Phase 20.7's Policy II (test.fail()-mark + follow-up micro phase) is the same discipline that produced this recheck. Each cross-demo scenario that can't meet the fixed tolerance becomes a tracked follow-up rather than a tolerance bump.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 20.7)

- **Playwright's `expect(buffer).toMatchSnapshot('a/b.png')` sanitizes `/` → `-` in the string form of its arg**. So the natural-looking `'cross-demo-baselines/kui/<id>.png'` resolves to a flat `cross-demo-baselines-kui-<id>.png` under the snapshot dir. The fix: pass the path as an **array** of segments (`['cross-demo-baselines', 'kui', '<id>.png']`) — Playwright joins them with the OS separator without sanitizing. This is documented but not prominent; first-encounter failure mode is "all 25 tests claim snapshot doesn't exist" while the file is actually present under a different path.
- **Cross-rendering body-element asymmetry**: chronix's `svg.cx-gantt-body` and k-ui's `.gantt-timeline-body-wrapper` are not dimensionally equivalent. Day-1 verify showed a consistent 1-px width / 3-px height offset across ALL 12 cross scenarios (8736×1315 vs 8737×1318). The two demos render to different wrapper element types (SVG vs div) with different border / padding / header-overlap semantics. Single root cause, not 12 regressions; tracked as Phase 20.7.1.
- **`maxDiffPixelRatio: 0` + `threshold: 0.2` is the strictest practical tolerance**. Zero ratio = no pixel may "differ"; threshold 0.2 (Playwright default) treats per-pixel RGB color distance ≤20% as same — absorbs sub-pixel AA noise on stroke edges and font hinting. Setting `threshold: 0` would force exact RGB match, virtually unachievable across SVG renderers. The combination caught the day-1 dimension offset cleanly (100% pixel diff on every cross scenario) and caught the fault-injection test (chronix bar background flipped from `#10b981` → `#ff0000`) on `vrt-week-themedBars` with clear diff PNG.
- **pnpm scripts + env vars on Windows**: cmd.exe (pnpm's default shell on Windows) doesn't accept the `KEY=VAL command` bash syntax. Avoiding a `cross-env` devDep for one var: tiny Node launcher `scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs` that sets the env explicitly and spawns playwright with stdio inherited. Per-script env (`CROSS_DEMO_CAPTURE` vs `CROSS_DEMO_RUN`) gates the corresponding spec's `test.skip` so neither runs during default `pnpm verify`.
- **Test gating via env var + `test.skip(!env)`**: both new spec files run as Playwright tests but `test.skip(!process.env['CROSS_DEMO_RUN'])` at the describe level inert them when the launcher hasn't set the var. This keeps `pnpm verify`'s default behavior unchanged — the 50 cross-demo tests (25 capture + 25 verify) show as "skipped" in the report but don't fail or extend runtime. The launcher pattern means the new scripts are 1-line aliases (`node scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs capture`).
- **Day-1 fail Policy II in practice**: 12-of-12 cross scenarios failing the same way pointed at a single root cause; the discipline says register the follow-up + mark `test.fail()` rather than bloat Phase 20.7's scope to fix it. The result: gate ships green (25 passed = 13 real + 12 test.fail()-passing) AND when 20.7.1 lands a fix, those 12 will report "Expected to fail, but passed" — the EXACT signal that the follow-up is complete and the marks should be removed.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 20.7)

- **Commit `4257932`** — design doc `audit/PHASE_20_7_CROSS_DEMO_SCREENSHOT_DIFF_DESIGN.md` (483 lines, 12-row catalog of infrastructure pieces). Three load-bearing decisions captured + resolved inline: A (`maxDiffPixelRatio: 0` + `threshold: 0.2`), B (25 scenarios split 12 cross + 13 vrt), C (frozen + manual k-ui baseline refresh). Day-1 baseline-fail Policy II (test.fail mark + follow-up micro phase) documented as the discipline.

- **Commit `8601e85`** — implementation Part 2: spec + scripts + baselines + skill update:

For each scenario, captures the REFERENCE side (k-ui for cross, chronix for vrt) and writes to `goldens/cross-demo-baselines/<subdir>/<id>.png` via `fs.writeFile`. Gated by `CROSS_DEMO_CAPTURE=true`.
  - `tooling/golden-runner/tests/cross-demo.spec.ts` (new, ~95 LOC): per-phase verify. Captures chronix-side, `expect(buffer).toMatchSnapshot([...segments], CROSS_DEMO_TOLERANCE)`. All 12 `kind: 'cross'` scenarios `test.fail()`-marked with Phase 20.7.1 reference (cross-demo body-region dimension mismatch). Gated by `CROSS_DEMO_RUN=true`.
  - `tooling/golden-runner/scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs` (new, ~37 LOC): cross-platform env-var launcher (`capture` / `verify` modes).

Handling docs for: regression detected, test.fail()-passing flip to green (follow-up phase done), k-ui upstream refresh.

**Fault-injection smoke test**: temporarily flipped `THEMED_BAR_BACKGROUND` from `#10b981` to `#ff0000` in `examples/gantt-vue3/src/sample-callbacks.ts`, re-ran verify. `vrt-week-themedBars` failed with a clear pixel diff. Reverted to `#10b981`, re-ran verify, 25/25 green again. Gate confirmed catches regressions.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 20.7)

- **Playwright's `toMatchSnapshot` slash-sanitizes string args**: first verify run reported all 25 as "snapshot doesn't exist" while the PNGs were physically present on disk — under a different path. Symptom: error says `Expected: goldens\cross-demo-baselines-kui-cross-week-default.png` (flat name) but capture wrote to `goldens\cross-demo-baselines\kui\cross-week-default.png` (nested). Fix: switch to the array-form arg `['cross-demo-baselines', 'kui', 'foo.png']` which Playwright joins without sanitizing.
- **First-run failed-verify auto-writes 12 stray PNGs**: when Playwright can't find a baseline for `toMatchSnapshot`, it writes the actual to the expected path AND fails the test. With the sanitized-path bug above, this left 12 flat-name PNGs in `goldens/` root that needed manual deletion before the fixed-path commit. Mitigation in future: verify path-resolution is correct via a one-scenario smoke test BEFORE running the full 25-scenario verify.
- **`cross-env` would have been simpler than a launcher script but adds a devDep** for setting one env var. The Node launcher is ~30 LOC + 1 mjs file. Trade was: smaller dep footprint vs more code in this repo. Smaller dep footprint won.
- **Pre-existing prettier format warning on `PHASE_20_6` design doc**: the design doc was authored before the pre-commit prettier hook landed (`b2d6280`) and had a "+" at line start that prettier interpreted as a list-item start. `pnpm format` auto-fixed it; included the fix in the Phase 20.7 commit since otherwise ci-check stays red. Noted in the commit body. Future authors: `pnpm format:check` locally before claiming docs done so pre-existing issues don't surface in later phases.
- **k-ui's view-toggle button cluster is INSIDE chart-root; chronix's is at page level**. `captureCrossDemoScreenshot` had to branch `toggleHost = source === 'kui' ? page.locator(CHART_SELECTOR) : page` to find the toggle. Discovered from re-reading the existing `visual.spec.ts` (uses chart-scoped getByRole) and `chronix-visual.spec.ts` (uses page-scoped getByRole) — they don't share helper code for this.

### Naming justifications (Phase 20.7)

- **`CrossDemoScenarioKind = 'cross' | 'vrt'`** — `'cross'` for "cross-demo (k-ui-vs-chronix) diff"; `'vrt'` for "chronix-only visual regression". Both 3-character codes keep the registry table readable in narrow markdown columns. Considered `'parity'` and `'self'` but `parity` already has heavy meaning in this codebase (DOM-level), and `'cross'` better signals the comparison is cross-side.
- **`CROSS_DEMO_TOLERANCE`** (vs `PIXEL_DIFF_TOLERANCE` or `SCREENSHOT_TOLERANCE`) — phase-scoped name signals "this is the tolerance for THE cross-demo registry", not a general-purpose tolerance constant. Future phases adding a different pixel-diff layer (e.g. interaction-replay screenshot diff) would get their own constant.
- **`captureCrossDemoScreenshot(source, browser, scenario)`** — 4-word name explicit about all 3 axes of variation: capture (the operation), cross-demo (the registry), screenshot (the output type). Returns `Buffer` (not a path) so the caller controls where it lands — capture spec writes via `fs.writeFile`, verify spec via `toMatchSnapshot`.
- **`hidePageChrome`** (vs `injectScreenshotCss` or `prepareForCapture`) — describes the user-visible effect (page chrome disappears) not the mechanism (CSS injection). Test authors needing to add another scenario just need to know "this hides chrome", not "this injects a style tag with these selectors".
- **`PENDING_CROSS_DIMENSION_FIX`** (vs `KNOWN_FAILING_SCENARIOS` or `TEST_FAIL_LIST`) — explicit about WHY: there's a pending fix (Phase 20.7.1) for a SPECIFIC root cause (dimension mismatch). When the fix lands and the Set is removed, future readers see why the marker existed.
- **`crossDemoBaselineRelPath`** (vs `baselinePath` or `getBaselinePath`) — returns a string path RELATIVE to the goldens dir. The "Rel" suffix flags this distinction; the unit-test asserts the exact relative form, callers join with their absolute base if needed.

### Open / parked (Phase 20.7)

- **Phase 20.7.1 — cross-demo body-region dimension fix**: all 12 `kind: 'cross'` scenarios fail day-1 with a uniform 1-px width / 3-px height offset. Chronix's `svg.cx-gantt-body` and k-ui's `.gantt-timeline-body-wrapper` are dimensionally inequivalent (different element types, different border/padding semantics). Two viable fixes documented in the spec file's header comment: (a) crop both sides to the calculated axis rect, or (b) switch chronix's capture target to a wrapper that includes the header band so wrapper-vs-wrapper matches apples-to-apples. Single follow-up phase covering all 12 marks. When 20.7.1 lands, Playwright will report `Expected to fail, but passed` on these 12, signaling the marks must be removed.
- **k-ui demo URL-config layer**: k-ui demo doesn't expose Phase 20.6's URL-config pattern, so cross scenarios with chronix-side URL flags rely on k-ui's default rendering already matching what those flags produce in chronix parity mode (e.g. `priorityCallback=true` in parity mode produces k-ui's default palette). Parked v2.x — adding URL-config to k-ui is upstream work and out of chronix's scope.
- **Cross-demo interaction replays** (drag a bar, screenshot after) — none yet. Lands with Phase 22 (toolbar) per the catalog in Phase 20.5's design doc.
- **Per-region diff masks** — none yet. Would let a scenario carve sub-regions where small known differences are tolerated. Current tolerance (`threshold: 0.2`) absorbs typical AA noise without needing masks; revisit if a Phase 21+ scenario truly needs sub-region control.
- **Larger-data scenarios** — current parity dataset is 25 bars × 32 rows. Cases with 500+ bars (chronix's design target for v2.x) not covered by these 25 scenarios.
- **Automated PNG diff visualizer** — Playwright already writes `<scenario>-diff.png` to `test-results/` on failure. No tooling to surface these in a gallery yet; manual `playwright show-report` is the current path.

## Phase 21 — todayLine (DONE, 2026-05-16)

First feature phase after the 20.5/20.6/20.7 infrastructure batch. Static vertical "today" line ported from k-ui — same `(Date.now() - axisStartMs) × pxPerMs` formula as `BarPlacementPass` so the line aligns pixel-exactly with bars starting today. Tooltip widget (red "今日" badge in header band). 3 stroke patterns (solid / dashed / dotted; k-ui's `double` + `dashed-dot` parked v0 — no clean SVG translation). API defaults to opt-in (`todayLine: false`); demo's parity mode auto-enables to match k-ui's rendered default. `nowIndicator` (5-min `setTimeout` + tab-visibility) explicitly NOT in scope per user direction. Phase 21 also served as the **infrastructure ROI test** for the 20.5+20.6+20.7 trio — see "Mechanisms understood" for the actual-vs-budgeted numbers.

### Reference reading (Phase 21)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:1110-1303` — `renderTodayLine()` method; `<div class="gantt-timeline-today-line">` div with `position: absolute; left: <todayX>; pointer-events: none; zIndex: 1.5`. Optional inner `<div>` for border-style line OR `<svg>` for dashed-dot pattern. Tooltip `<div class="gantt-timeline-today-line-tooltip">` with bg=color, white text, `zIndex: 4`, header-only.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/options-refiners.ts:8-13` — `TodayLineOption` shape: `{ color?, width?, tooltip?, style? }`. K-ui supports 5 styles (`solid` / `dashed` / `dotted` / `double` / `dashed-dot`); chronix v0 only the first 3.
- `d:/work/k-ui/examples/gantt/vue3/src/DemoApp.vue:1642-1661` — confirms upstream demo enables todayLine on by default with all defaults (`#ff6b6b`, 2 px, `dashed`, `今日`); 4 live-edit controls for color / width / style / tooltip text (chronix demo doesn't port these — single `?todayLine=true` URL flag only).
- `D:/work/chronix/packages/gantt/src/layout/bar-placement-pass.ts:21-22` — the canonical `(startMs - axisStartMs) × pxPerMs` formula. Phase 21 today-line uses the SAME math so bars and line are pixel-aligned.
- `D:/work/chronix/audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` lines 194-196 — sidebar dual-scrollport drift `🟡`. User surfaced the visual symptom during this session (k-ui sidebar has its own scrollbar, chronix wrapper has one combined). Promoted from "Park" to "Planned as Phase 23" in commit `9cde7e0` so the entry doesn't drift into forgotten state.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 21)

- **Single-source x-coord math is the right call**: by re-using `BarPlacementPass`'s formula for the today-line, the parity assertion came back at `Δ=0.00 px` on day-1 — pixel-perfect. If I'd written a separate "today position" computation, it'd have been one more drift source. The lesson generalizes: when a new render element shares a coordinate space with existing elements, reuse the existing math primitive — don't reinvent.
- **Vue 3 prop type for `T | boolean` union**: declaring `todayLine: { type: [Boolean, Object] as PropType<TodayLineOption | boolean>, default: false }` lets the consumer pass `false` (hide), `true` (all defaults), or `{...}` (per-field override). The runtime branch `opt === true ? {} : opt` normalizes inside `resolvedTodayLine`. Cleaner than splitting into two props (`enabled: bool` + `options: TodayLineOption`).
- **Theme-cascade decision — one prop drives both stroke + tooltip-bg**: k-ui's behavior is "one `color` knob controls both line stroke and tooltip background". Chronix mirrors via `tooltipBg = config.color ?? theme.todayLineTooltipBg`. When per-prop `color` is set → drives both; when unset → each falls back to its own theme token independently (so theme authors CAN diverge them, parity-reference consumers can't via prop). Best of both worlds.
- **Demo parity-mode wiring pattern**: chronix's parity mode (`?parity=true`) was already wiring 4 styling toggles (`themedBars`, `umbrellaColor`, `priorityCallback`, parity color) to k-ui-matching values. Phase 21 added a fifth (`activeTodayLine`) following the exact same pattern — `computed` that returns the enabled config when parity is on. The infrastructure is right; the cost is genuinely ~3 LOC per new toggle.
- **Playwright `--grep` over the launcher for targeted capture**: the original `pnpm cross-demo-capture` always re-captures ALL scenarios — dangerous when only adding 2. Forwarding extra args via the launcher (`node scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs capture --grep todayLine`) lets Phase 21+ phases capture only the NEW baselines without touching the 25 existing ones. Simple `process.argv.slice(3)` plus switching the spawn target to `pnpm exec playwright` (so it resolves outside `pnpm run`'s PATH).
- **`pxPerMs` for off-axis detection**: chronix renders `null` when `todayX < 0 || todayX > totalWidth`. K-ui's logic is the same (`return null` when today outside `normalizedRange`). Both behaviors match without extra translation — the formula is geometric, not framework-specific.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 21)

- **Commit `55e7c97`** — design doc `audit/PHASE_21_TODAY_LINE_DESIGN.md` (372 lines). 12-row catalog of k-ui surface with per-row disposition (✅ port / ⏸️ parked / ❌ rejected). 3 load-bearing decisions resolved: tooltip widget included; only 3 stroke styles; API opt-in + demo parity auto-enable.
- **Commit `9cde7e0`** — audit-only side commit (`PARITY_RECHECK.md` item #10-11): promoted "Park" → "Planned as Phase 23 (sidebar dual-scrollport)" so the surfaced drift doesn't drift into forgotten state.

  - `packages/gantt/src/api/gantt-options.ts`: `TodayLineOption` interface + `GanttOptions.todayLine` field with `TodayLineOption | boolean` type.

  - `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.test.ts`: +8 SFC tests in `describe('Phase 21 todayLine')` covering visibility, off-axis null, color/width props, all 3 stroke patterns, tooltip default/empty, theme fallback.

  - `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue`: 1 schema entry + `activeTodayLine` computed + 1 template prop binding.

  - `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts`: +1 cross-demo assertion (todayLine x-coordinate). **Day-1 result: kui=480.00 chronix=480.00 Δ=0.00 — pixel-perfect.**
  - `tooling/golden-runner/scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs`: arg-forward to playwright + switch to `pnpm exec` invocation.
  - 2 new chronix baselines captured via `node scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs capture --grep todayLine` (existing 25 untouched).

**Test count after Phase 21**:

**Infrastructure ROI assessment** (per design-doc Problem section):
The claim was each feature phase should add ~5 LOC parity assertion + 1-3 LOC demo toggle + 1-3 cross-demo scenarios. Actual for Phase 21:

- **DOM parity assertion (`parity.spec.ts`)**: ~50 LOC inline (kui-side eval + chronix-side eval + delta check + warn). Higher than 5-LOC target because Phase 20.5 helpers don't yet have a "single element x-coord extractor" — would need ~30 LOC added to `parity-helpers.ts` to make the call-site 5 LOC. **Verdict: partial ROI.** The infrastructure absorbed the bar/tick/header/sidebar surface; single-decoration extractors weren't generalized yet. Future phases (todayLine.x, nowIndicator-when-it-lands, grid-cell highlights) will reuse the inline pattern OR justify adding `extractDecorationsSnapshot` to `parity-helpers.ts`.
- **Demo toggle**: 1 schema line + 1 computed (~10 LOC) + 1 template line = ~12 LOC. **Verdict: ROI delivered.** Pre-20.6 the same toggle would have been ~30 LOC of hand-wired `ref` + `watch` + checkbox.
- **Cross-demo scenarios**: 2 registry entries (~14 LOC) + 2 count-bump test assertions. **Verdict: ROI delivered.** Capture + verify ran zero-friction via `pnpm cross-demo-capture --grep todayLine`; no spec file edits needed.
- **Total LOC**: 499 actual vs 265 estimate (+88%). Mostly absorbed by Commit 1's adapter render (~70 LOC of SVG primitives that has no infrastructure-level shortcut yet — every feature touching rendering pays this).

**Net assessment**: infrastructure paid off cleanly for demo toggles + cross-demo scenarios (3 LOC + 2 entries vs 30 LOC + bespoke spec). Did NOT pay off for DOM parity assertion at single-element granularity (would need a new helper). The 88% LOC overage is in adapter render — a feature-level cost, not infrastructure-fixable.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 21)

- **`@chronixjs/gantt` dist rebuild required twice**: first time when adding `TodayLineOption` import to adapter (`packages/gantt/dist` lagged source); second time after adding the `TodayLineOption` re-export to `packages/gantt/src/index.ts` (root re-export was missing). Memory rule `feedback_rebuild_dist_for_cross_package_changes.md` already documents this; Phase 21 was the 4th time this bites (after Phase 8 / 9 / 12). Possible future improvement: tsup `--watch` during adapter development.
- **`chronix-theme.test.ts`'s key-count assertion**: silent failure mode — adding theme tokens to `ChronixTheme` interface + `defaultChronixTheme` const passes adapter typecheck but breaks `chronix-theme.test.ts:54` (sorted-key equality). Caught by `pnpm ci-check` at the test step. Cheap to fix (2 entries in `EXPECTED_TOKEN_KEYS` + 2 in the `stringKeys` array) but the symptom message is obscure (diff output of two large key arrays). Could be improved with a "key was added: <list>" message.
- **Playwright `toMatchSnapshot` slash-sanitization was already known**, no re-hit this phase — Phase 20.7 fixed via array-form arg. The fix held for Phase 21's `--grep` capture flow.
- **`pnpm` vs raw `node` PATH resolution for `playwright`**: when invoked via `pnpm cross-demo-capture`, the launcher had `playwright` on PATH (via `pnpm run`'s synthesized PATH). When invoked via `node scripts/run-cross-demo.mjs capture --grep todayLine` (the new arg-forward path), PATH lacked `node_modules/.bin/playwright`. Fix: switch the launcher's `spawn` target to `pnpm exec playwright` so both invocation paths resolve. Doesn't break the existing `pnpm cross-demo-capture` flow.
- **Demo file edit risk to existing baselines**: even though Phase 21's `App.vue` edits are additive (new schema entry + new computed + new template prop), they could in principle have shifted unrelated bytes in the rendered DOM. Confirmed via `pnpm cross-demo-verify` that all 25 existing baselines pass unchanged after the edit — the additive changes don't leak into chronix-side rendering when the new flags are at default. Future phases should re-verify this each time the demo gets a new flag.

### Naming justifications (Phase 21)

- **`TodayLineOption`** (vs `TodayLineConfig` / `TodayLineProps`) — matches parity-reference's interface name verbatim, so a future codemod migrating users from upstream to chronix can rename only.
- **`resolvedTodayLine`** (vs `effectiveTodayLine` / `todayLineState`) — verb-prefix `resolved` matches the existing `resolveBarStyle` precedent in the codebase. The `null` return when off-axis or disabled is also "resolved" (to the inactive case).
- **`activeTodayLine`** (in App.vue, vs `effectiveTodayLine` / `computedTodayLine`) — matches the existing `activeBarColor` / `activeEventOverlap` etc. naming in App.vue for `computed`-driven props.
- **`todayLineColor` + `todayLineTooltipBg`** (vs `todayColor` + `todayBackgroundColor`) — `todayLine` prefix scopes them to the today-line feature unambiguously; `Tooltip` qualifier on the second token signals it's specifically the tooltip widget's background, not the whole-element background.
- **`data-today-line-side='body' | 'header'`** — DOM attribute on each rendered `<line>` so the cross-demo parity assertion can disambiguate the body-side line (which carries the canonical x-coord) from the header-side line (decorative). Without this, `document.querySelector('line.cx-gantt-today-line')` would return the first match (header — wrong frame for the assertion).
- **`TODAY_LINE` constant** in `reference-dom-map.ts` — matches the existing constant-naming convention (`EVENT_BAR`, `PROGRESS_TRIANGLE`, etc.) for upstream-DOM selectors.

### Open / parked (Phase 21)

- **`'double'` + `'dashed-dot'` stroke styles** — parked. K-ui supports both. `double` is a CSS-border idiom (two parallel lines) with no clean SVG translation; would need two `<line>` elements offset. `dashed-dot` requires custom dash pattern `8 4 2 4`. Both uncommon; revisit if a consumer reports needing them.
- **`nowIndicator`** — explicitly NOT in scope per user direction this session. Defer indefinitely. The k-ui 5-min `setTimeout` + tab-visibility + custom-render-hooks machinery is non-trivial; pulling it in just for parity coverage isn't justified without a real consumer use case.
- **Live midnight rollover** — Phase 21 `Date.now()` is sampled at render time only. A chart staying mounted across midnight won't auto-advance until the next reactive re-render. Acceptable v0; revisit if user reports.
- **Live-edit color / width / style / tooltip-text demo toggles** — k-ui demo has 4 controls; chronix demo has 1 (`?todayLine=true`). Live-edit color picker / style dropdown / tooltip text input parked — would expand demo by ~50 LOC for marginal feature-discovery value.
- **DOM parity helper for single-element decorations** — Phase 21 used inline `chart.evaluate` for the cross-demo today-line assertion (~50 LOC). The Phase 20.5 snapshot helpers are designed for sets of elements (bars / ticks / header cells); single decorations don't fit the pairing-by-id pattern. When Phase 22+ adds a second single-element decoration (grid-cell highlight? nowIndicator marker if it lands?), promote the inline pattern to `extractDecorationSnapshot('today-line' | '...', side)` in `parity-helpers.ts` to recover the ~5 LOC budget.
- **Phase 23 — sidebar dual-scrollport architecture** (allocated this session) — `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` item #10-11 promoted from "Park" to "Planned". Scope: split current single wrapper into two `overflow: auto` scrollports (sidebar + timeline body), add JS scroll-sync for vertical alignment, replace `position: sticky` header pinning with `translateX`-driven horizontal sync. ~6-8h single session. Will touch 5 chronix VRT baselines and likely require Phase 20.7 cross-demo baseline re-capture.
- **Next-session recommended audit-sweep** (per Phase 21 session discussion): pass over every `PARITY_RECHECK.md` 🟡 entry; classify each `Park` into `Planned (Phase X)` / `Defer-indefinite` / `Reject` with rationale. Estimated 1-2h. Without this, "parked" remains ambiguous about which items will eventually be fixed. NOT blocked on any other work; can run as its own small phase whenever.

## Phase 22 — Toolbar / view-switch buttons (DONE, 2026-05-16)

First chrome-layer phase. Lands `headerToolbar` prop on `<ChronixGantt>` with the parity-reference's string-DSL shape (`{ left: 'prev,next today', center: 'title', right: 'day,week,month,...' }`), parses it to a widget model, renders k-ui-parity class names, wires clicks through a controlled-prop `v-model:axis-input` pathway. Demo replaces its bare `cx-demo-view-toggle` block with the toolbar.

### Reference reading (Phase 22)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/Toolbar.tsx:1-73` — outer toolbar; section splitting (`left` forces LTR ordering; `start` respects RTL); class composition (`gantt-toolbar`, `gantt-toolbar-ltr`); three section render entry points.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/toolbar-parse.ts:39-173` — string-DSL → widget tree. Space-separated groups, comma-separated widgets per group. Widget name dispatch: `'title'` → marker, `customButtons[name]` → custom, `viewSpecs[name]` → view button (click calls `changeView(name)`), `api[name]` → nav button (click calls `api[name]()`). Hint formatter is `formatWithOrdinals` for nav button localization.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/ToolbarSection.tsx:6-147` — per-section render; inline SVG `<polyline>` icons for prev/next/prevYear/nextYear (no icon font dependency); `<button>` per widget with `aria-pressed`, `disabled` (from `isPrevEnabled` etc.), `gantt-<name>-button` + `theme.getClass('button')` + `'buttonActive'` classes.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/toolbar-struct.ts:1-66` — `ToolbarInput { left?, center?, right?, start?, end? }`, `ToolbarWidget`, `CustomButtonInput`, `ButtonIconsInput`, `ButtonTextCompoundInput` (i18n overrides for prev/next/today + view names), `ButtonHintCompoundInput` (aria-label overrides).
- `d:/work/k-ui/examples/gantt/vue3/src/DemoApp.vue:1346-1350` — canonical demo wiring `{ left: 'prev,next today', center: 'title', right: 'day,week,month,season,halfYear,year' }`. Custom `views[]` config commented out → view-button text falls back to FullCalendar English defaults.
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md:329` Disposition register Phase 22 row: "First phase needing button-click recording-replay parity (see Phase 20.5 catalog)" — recording-replay infra was promoted to Phase 22.1 follow-up.
- `audit/PHASE_20_5_PARITY_INFRASTRUCTURE_V2_DESIGN.md` catalog row "Interaction recording" parked v2.x for Phase 22.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 22)

- **String-DSL precedence**: `left` / `right` are LTR-locked aliases for `start` / `end`. When both forms appear on the same section, the LTR-locked value wins (matches reference's `Toolbar.tsx:30-42` precedence). Demo only uses `{ left, center, right }`; `start` / `end` accepted but unused.
- **View-button click = changeView semantics**: reference's `toolbar-parse.ts:120-122` wires `buttonClick = () => ganttSchedulerApi.changeView(buttonName)`. Chronix has no imperative `handle.changeView` yet (Phase 24); instead the toolbar emits `update:axisInput` with a new `viewId` field swapped in. Same end state (chart re-renders at new view), different mechanism (controlled prop vs imperative state mutation). Phase 24's imperative `handle.changeView` will compute-and-emit through the same internal pathway.
- **Nav-button click = `api[name]()` semantics**: reference's `toolbar-parse.ts:136-139` looks up the method on `ganttSchedulerApi` (e.g. `api.next()`) and wires it as the click handler. Chronix emits `update:axisInput` with a new `anchorDate` computed via per-view shifts (`day` ±1d, `week` ±7d, `month` ±1mo, `season` ±3mo, `halfYear` ±6mo, `year` ±1y).
- **Per-view label localization**: reference uses `buttonText` overrides for Chinese labels. Demo's `views: {}` config has Chinese `buttonText` commented out, so reference renders English `day`/`week`/etc. Chronix hard-codes Chinese `日`/`周`/`月`/`季`/`半年`/`年` in `parse-toolbar.ts:11-18` matching the existing `VIEW_TOGGLE` array in the demo template — drop-in for Chinese-locale consumers. i18n parking documented in catalog.
- **Title text format**: reference's title comes from `formatRange` (FullCalendar's locale-aware range formatter). Chronix's `formatToolbarTitle` uses fixed Chinese conventions (`YYYY-MM-DD`, `YYYY 第N周`, `YYYY年M月`, `YYYY Q1-4`, `YYYY H1/H2`, `YYYY年`). Both render NON-empty strings; format equality is parked with `buttonText` i18n.
- **`isPressed` derivation**: reference passes `activeButton: viewSpec.type` through `ToolbarSection.props.activeButton`. Chronix computes `isPressed: viewId === options.activeViewId` directly inside `parseToolbar` since the widget model is recomputed each render anyway.
- **Toolbar coordinate frame**: reference renders the toolbar at the top of `.gantt-scheduler`; chronix renders it inside a NEW `.cx-gantt-root` wrapper that sits between `.cx-demo-svg-frame` and `.cx-gantt-wrapper`. The bbox coordinate frame for `extractToolbarSnapshot` is toolbar-root-relative on BOTH sides, so cross-demo button-position parity works without normalizing chrome offsets.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 22)

- `packages/gantt/src/api/toolbar-types.ts` (new, 62 LOC): `ToolbarInput`, `ToolbarWidget`, `ToolbarWidgetKind`, `ToolbarModel`, `ParseToolbarOptions`. Flat shape (no nested groups) so callers can write a `ToolbarInput` literal inline.
- `packages/gantt/src/api/parse-toolbar.ts` (new, 124 LOC): `parseToolbar(input, options)` → `ToolbarModel`. Iterates `start/center/end` → space-split groups → comma-split widgets → dispatch by name. Throws on unknown widget with a message naming the accepted alternatives (`title | day/week/.../year | prev/next/today`).
- `packages/gantt/src/api/nav-utils.ts` (new, 105 LOC): `nextAnchor` / `prevAnchor` per `viewId`; `todayAnchor()` returns local-midnight Date; `formatToolbarTitle(axisInput)` for title text (Chinese-locale defaults; locale-driven `Intl.DateTimeFormat` is future-phase scope).
- `packages/gantt/src/api/chronix-theme.ts` (+6 tokens, +25 LOC): `toolbarBg` / `toolbarButtonBg` / `toolbarButtonBgActive` / `toolbarButtonBorder` / `toolbarButtonColor` / `toolbarTitleColor`. Default palette matches existing chronix chrome (neutral grayscale + bar-blue accent for pressed).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (+230 LOC): new `headerToolbar` prop (`ToolbarInput | false`, default `false`); new `update:axisInput` emit; computed `toolbarModel` / `toolbarTitleText`; `onToolbarWidgetClick` handler routes view-click → `viewId` swap, nav-click → `anchorDate` shift; module-level `renderToolbar` / `renderToolbarSection` / `renderToolbarWidgetGroup` / `renderToolbarButton` / `renderToolbarIcon` h() helpers. Render wraps the existing `.cx-gantt-wrapper` in a new `.cx-gantt-root` parent when toolbar enabled; returns the bare wrapper otherwise (backward-compat).
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue` (~30 LOC delta): drop bare `.cx-demo-view-toggle` + 6-button block + `VIEW_TOGGLE` array. Add local `anchorDate` ref + `axisInput` computed reads it; `HEADER_TOOLBAR` literal wired through `:header-toolbar`; `@update:axis-input="onUpdateAxisInput"` splits the emitted axisInput back to `cfg.view` + `anchorDate`.
- `tooling/golden-runner/src/parity-helpers.ts` (+110 LOC): `ToolbarWidgetSnapshot` interface + `extractToolbarSnapshot(source, page)` helper. Multi-element pairing by `buttonName` extracted from `(?:cx-)?gantt-<name>-button` class regex; per-widget `kind: title | view | nav | unknown` classification; bbox relative to toolbar root.
- `tooling/golden-runner/src/reference-dom-map.ts` (+22 LOC): `TOOLBAR_ROOT` / `TOOLBAR_TITLE` / `TOOLBAR_BUTTON_CLASS_PATTERN` constants.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+3 assertions, +130 LOC): toolbar button set / active-button / title presence cross-demo parity. **All 3 PASS against live demos** (chronix at 8702, k-ui at 8701). Active-button assertion confirms both sides show `aria-pressed='true'` on the `week` button after `loadBothDemos`' standard `周` click; widget-set assertion confirms 10 expected ids (`title` + 3 nav + 6 view) appear on both sides.

**Test count after Phase 22**:

- vitest: 445 → **483** (+38). Core 240→267 (+27 = 12 parseToolbar + 15 nav-utils); adapter 194→205 (+11 toolbar SFC); demo 11 unchanged.
- golden-runner Playwright unit tests: 32 unchanged (count assertions stable).
- parity.spec.ts: 28 → **31** assertions (+3 toolbar).
- cross-demo scenarios: 27 unchanged (12 cross + 15 vrt). 27/27 cross-demo-verify gate green after 15 chronix-self VRT baselines re-captured for 1-pixel height shift introduced by `.cx-gantt-root` wrapper.
- 5 chronix VRT baselines + 6 k-ui parity goldens + 17 chronix-visual baselines: unchanged.
- **15 chronix cross-demo baselines updated** (1-pixel height shift from toolbar above wrapper).

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 22)

- **1-pixel layout shift on chronix-self VRT baselines**: adding `.cx-gantt-root` as a new wrapper between `.cx-demo-svg-frame` and `.cx-gantt-wrapper` shifted the rendered SVG body's bbox by 1 vertical pixel (171→172px in the test capture). Existing 15 chronix-self VRT baselines failed strict-pixel-perfect tolerance. Bars + today-line render at IDENTICAL horizontal positions; only the outer frame's vertical extent shifted. Re-baseline was the right call (toolbar is now part of the canonical chronix demo render). 12 k-ui-baseline cross scenarios stayed green throughout — k-ui side is unchanged.
- **`noUncheckedIndexedAccess` strict typing**: `parse-toolbar.test.ts` initially used `model.sectionWidgets.start[0].map(...)` — failed core typecheck because `[0]` returns `T | undefined`. Fixed with `!` non-null assertions on each indexed access. Same lesson as Phase 21's `chronix-theme.test.ts` `EXPECTED_TOKEN_KEYS` discipline — TS strict mode catches array-index drift; embrace the `!` for known-length test fixtures.
- **prettier hook reformatted Decision-3 table**: design doc commit (`7e12b47`) had wide markdown tables; prettier expanded column widths post-commit. Hook detected the formatting in pre-commit, accepted the reformat. No content change.
- **eslint import-order auto-fix needed twice**: the type imports for `ToolbarInput` / `ToolbarModel` / `ToolbarWidget` / `ViewId` and the runtime `parseToolbar` / `nextAnchor` / etc were initially in the wrong order per `import-x/order`. `pnpm exec eslint --fix` cleaned them up; would have failed CI otherwise.
- **`as ToolbarInput` redundant cast caught by `@typescript-eslint/no-unnecessary-type-assertion`**: my initial `parseToolbar(input as ToolbarInput, ...)` was redundant since TS already narrowed `input` to `ToolbarInput | undefined` (then guard ruled out `undefined`). Just removed the cast.
- **`@chronixjs/gantt` dist rebuild required**: 5th time this bites since Phase 8. Pre-flight checklist worked — ran `pnpm --filter @chronixjs/gantt build` BEFORE adapter typecheck. ci-check would have caught it; cheaper to remember up front.
- **`chronix-theme.test.ts`'s key-count assertion (Phase 21 gotcha repeat avoided)**: added 6 toolbar tokens to `EXPECTED_TOKEN_KEYS` + 6 to `stringKeys` array. Pre-flight checklist worked.

### Naming justifications (Phase 22)

- **`ToolbarInput`** (vs `ToolbarConfig` / `HeaderToolbar`): matches the parity-reference's verbatim interface name (`d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/toolbar-struct.ts:16`) so a future codemod migrating users from upstream to chronix can rename imports only.
- **`ToolbarWidgetKind`** (vs `ToolbarItemType` / `WidgetClass`): "widget kind" matches the existing `kind:` discriminator convention chronix uses elsewhere (`CrossDemoScenarioKind`, etc.). "Item" was rejected because `<button>` and `<h2>` are widgets, not items.
- **`parseToolbar`** (vs `buildToolbarModel` / `compileHeaderToolbar`): matches reference's `parseToolbar` function name verbatim (`d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/toolbar-parse.ts:8`).
- **`nextAnchor` / `prevAnchor` / `todayAnchor`** (vs `addPeriod` / `subPeriod`): the function returns a new ANCHOR DATE specifically (the `axisInput.anchorDate` field), not just any date arithmetic. `nextAnchor` reads as "the anchor date for the next view-period" which is exactly what the toolbar emits.
- **`formatToolbarTitle`** (vs `formatRangeTitle` / `computeToolbarTitle`): "format" + "title" matches the function's role (string formatting for the title widget). "Range" was rejected because the function takes the full `AxisRangePlanInput`, not just the range — `viewId` also drives the format selection.
- **`cx-gantt-root`** (vs `cx-gantt-shell` / `cx-gantt-frame`): "root" matches the existing chronix naming convention (the wrapper IS the root of the gantt component tree when toolbar is present). Distinct from `cx-gantt-wrapper` which now denotes specifically the chart's scroll-port.
- **`data-button-name` + `data-button-kind`** (custom data-attrs on toolbar buttons): named after the `ToolbarWidget.buttonName` + `kind` fields so the parity extractor's regex-based name derivation + kind classification can also be done via `data-*` lookup if class-name parsing becomes flaky. Belt-and-suspenders; both used in `extractToolbarSnapshot`.
- **`extractToolbarSnapshot`** (vs `extractToolbar` / `snapshotToolbar`): matches the Phase 20.5 `extract*Snapshot` helper naming convention (`extractBarsSnapshot`, `extractTicksSnapshot`, `extractSidebarSnapshot`, `extractHeaderCellsSnapshot`).
- **`toolbarBg` / `toolbarButtonBg{Active}` / `toolbarButtonBorder` / `toolbarButtonColor` / `toolbarTitleColor`** (6 theme tokens): all `toolbar`-prefixed for token-namespace clarity; flat shape matching the rest of `ChronixTheme` (no nested `toolbar: { ... }`).

### Open / parked (Phase 22)

- **Phase 22.1 — toolbar click recording-replay infrastructure** (~3-4h): Phase 20.5 catalog promoted "Interaction recording (pointer gestures captured + replayed)" to land with Phase 22. v0 parity in this phase uses static DOM snapshots; the recording-replay infrastructure (Playwright launcher → JSON event log → replay step-by-step → per-step DOM diff) is its own follow-up phase. Trigger: whenever a second phase needs button-click parity (Phase 24 imperative API → `handle.next()` invocation + assert post-state DOM); fold both into 22.1 then.
- **Cross-demo VRT toolbar-element scenarios** (3 scenarios per design doc): refined OUT of Phase 22 scope. The 3 design-doc scenarios (`vrt-toolbar-default-week`, `vrt-toolbar-after-view-change-month`, `vrt-toolbar-after-next`) would have required extending `CrossDemoScenario` with an optional `captureSelector` field (currently hard-coded to body wrapper). The 3 parity-spec assertions + 11 SFC tests already cover toolbar drift; the captureSelector extension is a Phase 22.1 add IF a toolbar visual regression slips through.
- **`buttonText` / `buttonHints` i18n** — defer to a future i18n phase that does `Intl.DateTimeFormat` properly for title text too.
- **`footerToolbar`** — port pathway is identical to header (~30 LOC delta). Land when a consumer wires it.
- **Year-nav buttons (`prevYear` / `nextYear`)** — demo doesn't use; defer-indefinite.
- **`customButtons`** — defer to first consumer request.
- **`validRange` + `isPrevEnabled` / `isNextEnabled` / `isTodayEnabled`** — defer until validRange becomes a phase.
- **`viewSpec.buttonTextOverride` / `buttonTitleOverride`** — defer with i18n.
- **`<ChronixGanttToolbar>` as standalone component** — current monolithic approach matches k-ui's chrome model. Split if a consumer needs toolbar placement elsewhere.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 22)

Design-doc estimate: ~650 LOC across 2 implementation commits. Actual:

- Commit 1 (`7935b74`): 982 LOC across 11 files (5 new core + adapter + theme + index + tests). ~50% overage; absorbed by the inline `renderToolbar` / `renderToolbarSection` / `renderToolbarWidgetGroup` / `renderToolbarButton` / `renderToolbarIcon` h() factories which were 180 LOC larger than the design's "render layer" estimate.
- Commit 2 (`099cb5a`): 286 LOC + 15 baseline updates. Design estimated ~120 LOC of `extractToolbarSnapshot` + 3 parity assertions; actual ~110 LOC for the extractor + ~130 LOC for the 3 parity-spec tests + ~46 LOC for demo wiring delta. On budget.

**Verdict**: SFC + parity-helper infrastructure paid off cleanly (extractor follows Phase 20.5's `extract*Snapshot` pattern, 3 parity assertions fit in <150 LOC total). Adapter render LOC was the overage source — Phase 21 saw the same pattern (every feature touching SVG/h() render pays a fixed render-LOC cost; no infrastructure shortcut). Demo toggle infrastructure also paid off (cfg.view reused, no schema change needed).

## Phase 22-AUDIT — silent-gap sweep (audit-only, 2026-05-16)

User found `todayBgColor` (k-ui yellow today-column tint) as a feature in the parity reference that had NO chronix catalog row and NO `PARITY_RECHECK.md` disposition row. Trust statement: "我现在不信任你 [I don't trust you right now]". This sweep responds by enumerating the entire k-ui public surface (~350 items across 7 source families) and classifying each against chronix's current state to find every comparable silent gap.

### Reference reading (Phase 22-AUDIT)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/options.ts` — full `GanttSchedulerOptions` enumeration (211 option names extracted via parallel `Explore` agent dispatch)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/theme/{GlobalThemeOverrides,applyThemeOverrides,Theme}.ts` + CSS variable greps (29 theme tokens: 27 typed + 2 CSS-only)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/api/structs.ts` + per-feature `*ContentArg.ts` (63 slot/content arg shapes, ~380 fields total)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/api/GanttSchedulerImpl.ts` (33 imperative API methods)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/structs/view-spec.ts` (10 view-spec fields)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/**/*.css` + DOM emitters (~40 consumer-targetable CSS classes + data attributes)
- `d:/work/k-ui/examples/gantt/vue3/src/DemoApp.vue:1343-1500` (~50 demo wiring items, mostly overlap with options)

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 22-AUDIT)

- **The discipline gap is architectural, not authorial**: `feedback_no_logic_drift_from_kui.md` requires every k-ui sub-behavior to have an explicit disposition (`done` / `parked` / `rejected`). The rule was enforced by human author care during PHASE\_\*\_DESIGN.md writing — author lists items they're thinking about that day; adjacent surface items get silently skipped. No tooling caught this.
- **Parallels exist for analogous discipline gaps**: `feedback_chronix_parity_discipline.md` describes the same human-only-enforcement pattern for parity assertions, solved by `/phase-close` skill + parity-spec regex check. The catalog rule is the unprotected sibling.
- **Cluster compression**: 170 silent-gap items would balloon disposition register from ~38 rows to 200+. Clustering by feature family (e.g. "all-day cluster" subsumes 8 options + 3 arg shapes + 1 CSS class + 3 default-value options under ONE Reject rationale) compresses to ~22 cluster rows + ~12 individuals. Each cluster row enumerates member names inline so the auto-scanner can substring-match each k-ui name.
- **Substring-match vs strict-table-row parsing**: a strict markdown parser would reject `` `eventOverlap` `` (backtick-wrapped) as not-a-table-row. Substring match accepts ANY mention as "considered". False-positive risk (a typo / commented-out / reject-rationale mention counts as covered) is the lesser evil vs false-negative (silent gap → drift).

### Chronix work derived (Phase 22-AUDIT)

- `audit/SILENT_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md` (new, ~942 lines): enumeration + 5-way classification (✅ done+cataloged / ⚠ done+uncataloged / 🔴 silent gap / ⏸️ cataloged-parked-no-disposition / ❌ rejected) of every k-ui surface item. Per-cluster tables in Sections A.1 through G.
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` (expanded ~370 lines): new "Silent-gap sweep additions (audit-sweep 2026-05-16)" section. Adds:
  - ~12 individual silent-gap dispositions (`todayBgColor` → Planned Phase 22.2, `selectMinDistance` → Phase 25 scope, `initialDate` / `initialView` / `dateIncrement` / `incrementDate` / `getDate` / `zoomTo` → Phase 24, `prevYear` / `nextYear` / `validRange` → Defer-indefinite + trigger, `now` / `themeSystem` → Reject)
  - ~22 cluster dispositions (toolbar i18n / event lifecycle hooks / editing granularity / touch / external drag-in / time bounds / explicit sizing / day-header customization / slot-label customization / week-numbers / all-day → Reject / event sources / resource hooks / popover / background events / selection theming / hover button theming / edge-resizer theming / a11y hints / per-view config / custom rendering meta / formatter API / initial scroll / window resize / etc)
  - ~36 uncataloged-but-done backfills (Phase 4-22 items chronix has but lacked explicit catalog rows: `unselectAuto`, `slotRegistry`, `theme` prop, `sticky-header`, `locale`, `rows`, `LinkSpec.routing`, payload-type aliases, full CSS class taxonomy)
  - 6 alias / variant entries surfaced by Phase 22.AUTOMATE's first scanner run (`EventResizeStartArg` / `EventResizeStopArg` / `EventProgressStartArg` / `EventProgressStopArg` / `EventReceiveLeaveArg` / `viewClassNames` / `nowIndicatorWillUnmount` / `eventAdd` / `eventRemove`)

## Phase 22.AUTOMATE — catalog-completeness CI gate (DONE, 2026-05-16)

Direct response to the silent-gap discipline-gap finding. Moves catalog discipline from human-authored to CI-enforced.

### Reference reading (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- `scripts/check-banned-names.mjs` — existing analogous gate, used as pattern reference (banned-identifier scanner, run via `pnpm audit:names`, wired into `ci-check`)
- `scripts/check-no-external-repo-refs.mjs` — analogous pre-commit hook (different enforcement model — PreToolUse, not CI)
- `package.json` — `ci-check` script chain pattern (format / lint / typecheck / test / build / audit:names → extended to 7th step)
- `audit/SILENT_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md` — source of baseline JSON enumeration

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- **Frozen baseline approach**: parsing `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/options.ts` at every CI run would add k-ui as a hard chronix-CI dependency (fragile when k-ui is moved/renamed). Instead, `audit/KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE.json` captures a frozen enumeration. New k-ui surface items get added to baseline manually when discovered; CI then enforces they have dispositions.
- **Markdown corpus scanning is sufficient**: every chronix audit document is markdown under `audit/**`. Concatenating all `audit/**/*.md` contents into one corpus + substring-matching baseline items against it is O(N×M) but tiny in practice (32 audit files × 359 baseline items × ~100KB total corpus = milliseconds).
- **Defensive: baseline JSON excluded by extension filter**: the scanner reads `*.md` only, so the baseline JSON (which lists every k-ui name) can't "self-satisfy" by listing items it's about to flag.
- **Test fixture strategy**: vitest config doesn't reach `scripts/` (outside workspace packages). A standalone `.test.mjs` matches the `check-banned-names.mjs` pattern — zero-dep, executable, uses `execFileSync` + temp-fixture dirs for fail cases.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- `audit/KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE.json` (new, 359 items across 6 surfaces): `options` (198), `theme` (27), `args` (63), `api` (27), `viewSpec` (3 — only the truly view-spec-specific fields; `type`/`component`/`buttonText`/etc. cataloged under options surface), `cssClasses` (35).
- `scripts/audit-catalog-completeness.mjs` (new, ~125 LOC): recursive `audit/**/*.md` discovery, baseline JSON load, substring-match per item, per-surface grouped error output, exit-1 with actionable "Fix:" message.
- `scripts/audit-catalog-completeness.test.mjs` (new, ~220 LOC, 5 cases): scan-clean, baseline-parse, surface-completeness, fail-on-missing, group-by-surface. Uses `mkdtempSync` + `execFileSync` for fail-case temp fixtures.
- `package.json` (modified): `audit:catalog` + `audit:catalog-test` scripts; `ci-check` chain extended to 7 steps.
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` (modified): added the 6-alias backfill paragraph that the first scanner run identified as missing.

**Verified outcomes**:

- `pnpm audit:catalog` → exit 0, "359 k-ui items across 6 surfaces; 32 audit files scanned"
- `pnpm audit:catalog-test` → 5/5 cases pass
- `pnpm ci-check` → fully green with new 7th step
- First scanner run identified 9 alias / variant names I'd missed in dispositions; added a "Alias / variant names" subsection to PARITY_RECHECK; re-scan passed.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- **`node:fs/promises` `glob` not available in node 20 LTS**: initial draft tried `import { glob }` from `node:fs/promises`. Available only in node 22+ as `fs.promises.glob`. Refactored to a manual recursive `readdir({ withFileTypes: true })` walker — works on node 20+ matching the repo's `engines.node: ">=20"` constraint.
- **Test-fixture exit-code parsing**: `execFileSync` throws on non-zero exit. Wrapped in try/catch to extract `err.stdout` / `err.stderr` / `err.status` for failure assertions. Same pattern as Phase 22 demo's earlier test scaffolding.
- **Self-satisfaction risk (defensive)**: the baseline JSON lists every k-ui name. If the scanner reads `*.json` too, it would self-satisfy by reading its own baseline. Extension filter to `.md` only blocks this; defensive comment in the scanner.
- **First-run discovery of 9 missing aliases**: scanner exposed that PARITY_RECHECK didn't explicitly name 9 variant / alias k-ui types (`EventResizeStartArg` distinct from `EventResizeStartStopArg`, etc.). Validates the gate's value — caught real missing dispositions on initial deployment. Documented as a "Alias / variant" subsection.
- **No `viewSpec.classNames` / `content` / `didMount` / `willUnmount` in baseline**: these names collide with top-level options of the same name (e.g. `viewClassNames` vs view-spec inheritor's `classNames`). The baseline includes only view-spec-UNIQUE names (`buttonTextKey`, `dateProfileGeneratorClass`, `usesMinMaxTime`); cross-cutting inheritance is dispositioned at the top-level option entries. Trade-off: granularity loss for zero false positives.

### Naming justifications (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- **`KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE.json`** (vs `kui-surface-baseline.json` / `surface-baseline.json`): matches the screaming-snake-case convention chronix already uses for `BANNED_IDENTIFIERS.md`, `R2_MAPPING.md`, `PARITY_RECHECK.md`, `SILENT_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md`. Signals "audit-critical artifact, not casual config".
- **`audit:catalog`** (vs `audit:gaps` / `audit:silent` / `audit:coverage`): matches the `audit:names` sibling pattern. "Catalog" maps to the per-PHASE catalog-table concept that this script enforces presence-in.
- **`audit-catalog-completeness.mjs`** (vs `check-catalog-coverage.mjs`): "audit-" prefix signals it's part of the chronix audit infrastructure (sibling to the `audit/` directory + `audit:*` scripts). "completeness" specifies what aspect is being checked.
- **`scan clean`** in success message: matches the `banned-identifier scan clean (140 files)` format used by `check-banned-names.mjs`. Consistent UX across the two gates.
- **5-way classification (✅ / ⚠ / 🔴 / ⏸️ / ❌)**: ⚠ for done-but-uncataloged was added beyond the existing 4-way disposition register because uncataloged-dones are a distinct class — they're working code but discipline gaps. 🔴 for silent gap is the urgent class. ⏸️ collapsed to "cataloged-parked but no register row" since the parked-no-disposition pattern is its own discipline gap.

### Open / parked (Phase 22.AUTOMATE)

- **Word-boundary match (`\beventOverlap\b`)** as a follow-up if false positives become a problem. Substring is the v0 default for false-negative minimization.
- **Strict table-row parser** rejected. Too brittle (markdown tables render different across linters; backtick-wrapping breaks naïve cell extraction).
- **Auto-regenerate baseline from k-ui source** — rejected for v0 (parsing TS source requires `ts-morph` or similar; adds a 5MB+ dependency). Manual baseline update on k-ui bump is the simpler maintenance model. Re-evaluate if baseline drift becomes a real issue.
- **Cross-language enforcement** — currently k-ui-only baseline. Future packages (`@chronixjs/table`, `@chronixjs/input`) would each need their own baseline JSON. The script generalizes trivially (`audit/<package>-baseline.json` pattern).
- **CI parallelization** — `ci-check` runs sequentially. `audit:catalog` is fast (~50ms) so adding it as a parallel turbo task isn't worth the wiring complexity. Stays serial after `audit:names`.

## Phase 22.AUTOMATE — DONE

- 2 commits: `dbb3c36` (design doc, 154 lines) + `bcb0c44` (Commit 1: baseline JSON + scanner + tests + wiring + 6-alias backfill, 745 lines).
- **No vitest delta** (script self-test is standalone, not registered with workspace vitest). Cumulative vitest still **483/483**.
- **No parity-spec delta** (chronix-new declaration; gate is infrastructure not k-ui feature port). Cumulative parity assertions still **31**.
- **No cross-demo delta** (no DOM change). 27/27 cross-demo-verify green.
- **+1 ci-check step**: `pnpm audit:catalog` now 7th in the chain. **359 k-ui items × 32 audit files** scanned at every CI run.
- **5/5 self-test cases pass**.
- `/phase-close` skill walked all 6 gates green (no cross-demo-verify needed — no DOM impact).
- **Effect**: any future PHASE\_\*\_DESIGN.md that ships without dispositioning a k-ui surface item — or any new k-ui surface item added to baseline without a chronix disposition — fails CI. The silent-gap class that broke trust on 2026-05-16 is now structurally prevented.

## Phase 22.2 — todayLine default-ON + todayBgColor (DONE, 2026-05-16)

Bundles the two user-found visible-parity gaps from the 2026-05-16 evening session:

1. `todayLine` was implemented in Phase 21 but chronix demo defaults OFF while parity-reference defaults ON.
2. `todayBgColor` was the user-found silent gap that triggered the audit-sweep + Phase 22.AUTOMATE.

### Reference reading (Phase 22.2)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/theme/GlobalThemeOverrides.ts:81` — `todayBgColor?: string` typed surface
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/theme/applyThemeOverrides.ts:32` — `todayBgColor → --gantt-today-bg-color` CSS-variable map
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:525-537` — header-side today rect emit (`gantt-timeline-header-cell-today` class)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:950-961` — body-side today rect emit (`gantt-today-highlight` class)
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/component/date-rendering.ts:40` — `gantt-day-today` (DIFFERENT path — month-view day cells, NOT the timeline-body today tint)
- `d:/work/k-ui/examples/gantt/vue3/src/DemoApp.vue:1339` — demo wires `todayBgColor: 'rgba(255, 220, 40, .15)'`

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 22.2)

- **k-ui emits today-tint via TWO distinct render paths**: header-side as one `<rect class="gantt-timeline-header-cell-today">` per header cell that overlaps today, body-side as ONE `<rect class="gantt-today-highlight">` per visible row PER HOUR-SLOT of today (24 rects per row in week view since each slot is 1 hour). Chronix's single full-day rect spans the same union extent (1248 px in week view) but as ONE rect not 24×N.
- **`.gantt-day-today` is NOT the body-tint class**: the original audit-sweep's reference-DOM-map entry (Section F of SILENT_GAP_SWEEP) was incorrect. `.gantt-day-today` is `date-rendering.ts:40` — a month-VIEW per-day-cell class, NOT the timeline-body tint. Caught when the first parity-assertion run found 0 elements matching `.gantt-day-today` in the body wrapper. Corrected in PARITY_RECHECK + reference-dom-map.
- **chronix vs k-ui slot model is hourly in both day + week**: chronix's `planWeekView` emits `slotDurationMs: MS_PER_HOUR` with `slotCount = 24 × 7 = 168`. K-ui does the same. So chronix's day-cell width = `MS_PER_DAY × pxPerMs` = `24 × slotWidth` = 1248 px. K-ui paints 24 individual 52-px rects covering the same 1248-px span. The parity assertion compares union extent (min-left → max-right) on the k-ui side against chronix's single-rect bbox — exact pixel match.
- **Header rect z-order**: chronix renders header-side today-cell rect AFTER `headerRowChildren` (so outer month/week band backgrounds paint first) but BEFORE `axis` tick labels (so labels stay legible). Matches k-ui's visual layering.
- **Body rect z-order**: chronix renders body-side today-cell rect BEFORE `todayLineBodyNode` and BEFORE bars (so bars + line paint on top). Matches k-ui's body-side rendering where bars are foreground.
- **`activeTodayCellBg` mirrors `activeTodayLine` pattern**: parity-mode auto-enables (`cfg.parity.value ? {} : ...`); standalone URL flag still works (`?todayCellBg=false` to disable). Same wiring as Phase 21.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 22.2)

- `packages/gantt/src/api/gantt-options.ts`: new `TodayCellBgOption { color?: string }` interface mirroring `TodayLineOption`'s shape
- `packages/gantt/src/api/chronix-theme.ts`: new `todayCellBgColor` theme token; default `'rgba(255, 220, 40, .15)'` matches parity-reference byte-for-byte
- `packages/gantt/src/api/chronix-theme.test.ts`: bumped `EXPECTED_TOKEN_KEYS` + `stringKeys` (+1, 41-token surface)
- `packages/gantt/src/api/index.ts` + `packages/gantt/src/index.ts`: re-export `TodayCellBgOption`
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts`: new `todayCellBg` prop, new `resolvedTodayCellBg` computed (today-local-midnight + clamped-to-axis-bounds), new `todayCellBodyNode` + `todayCellHeaderNode` render functions, threaded into body SVG (before bars) + header SVG (after headerRows, before axis)
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.test.ts`: `describe('Phase 22.2 todayCellBg')` with 6 SFC tests (default-hidden, body+header render, color prop override, theme fallback, default color, out-of-axis suppression)
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue`: flipped `todayLine` default `false → true`; added `todayCellBg` schema (default true); new `activeTodayCellBg` computed mirroring `activeTodayLine`; wired `:today-cell-bg` on `<ChronixGantt>`
- `tooling/golden-runner/src/reference-dom-map.ts`: new `TODAY_CELL_BODY` (`.gantt-today-highlight`) + `TODAY_CELL_HEADER` (`.gantt-timeline-header-cell-today`) constants
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts`: new cross-demo today-cell parity assertion using union-extent extraction on k-ui side
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md`: `todayBgColor` row promoted `Planned → DONE Phase 22.2`; corrected class attribution
- `audit/KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE.json`: +2 CSS classes; catalog-completeness scanner 359 → 361 items
- 15 chronix-self cross-demo VRT baselines re-captured

**Test count after Phase 22.2**:

- vitest: 483 → **489** (+6 SFC `chronix-gantt.test.ts` Phase 22.2 todayCellBg). Core 267, adapter 205→211, demo 11.
- golden-runner Playwright unit tests: 32 unchanged.
- parity.spec.ts: 31 → **32** assertions (+1 todayCellBg). **Δ=0.00 — pixel-perfect**.
- cross-demo scenarios: 27 unchanged. 27/27 cross-demo-verify green.
- KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE: 359 → 361 items, catalog scan clean.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 22.2)

- **`.gantt-day-today` mis-attribution in SILENT_GAP_SWEEP**: audit-sweep listed `.gantt-day-today` as the body-side today-tint class. First parity-assertion run found 0 elements. Grep on k-ui revealed body class is actually `.gantt-today-highlight` (`GanttView.tsx:959`); `.gantt-day-today` is month-view-only. Audit-sweep produced an incorrect reference-DOM-map entry; corrected in this phase. Meta-lesson: even the silent-gap audit can have its own silent gaps; runtime parity assertions catch them where catalog-completeness scan cannot.
- **k-ui paints today-bg as 24 hourly rects in week view, not one daily rect**: initial parity assertion compared the FIRST k-ui rect (52 px wide, one hour) against chronix's single-day rect (1248 px). Width delta 1196 px (24×). Fix: union extent (min-left + max-right across all matching rects) on k-ui side. Lesson: when k-ui's slot model is finer-grained than chronix's per-feature rendering, extract aggregate geometry not first-element geometry.
- **VRT layout shift cascading from Phase 22 to Phase 22.2**: Phase 22 already re-captured 15 chronix-self VRT baselines for the toolbar wrapper's 1-px height shift. Phase 22.2's new today-cell rect adds visible pixels to those same 15 baselines. All 15 re-captured a second time — total VRT update count for the day = 15 + 15 = 30 captures across 2 phases.
- **`noUncheckedIndexedAccess` strict on querySelectorAll loop**: the parity-assertion's k-ui-side evaluate callback initially used `const cell = cells[0]`. TS strict mode flagged "possibly undefined". Fixed with `if (!cell) return null` guard.

### Naming justifications (Phase 22.2)

- **`todayCellBg`** (prop name, vs `todayBgColor` matching k-ui verbatim): "CellBg" matches chronix's existing `todayLine` precedent — feature-prefix + descriptor. Symmetric naming makes the two today-feature props read together (`todayLine`, `todayCellBg`). K-ui's `todayBgColor` smushes "Bg" + "Color"; chronix's option is an object `{ color?: string }` matching `TodayLineOption`'s shape.
- **`todayCellBgColor`** (theme token, vs `todayCellBg`): adds the `Color` suffix to disambiguate from the prop. Matches `todayLineColor` precedent.
- **`.cx-gantt-today-cell`** (CSS class, vs `.cx-gantt-today-bg`): "cell" is the noun (it IS a cell); `data-today-cell-side='body|header'` matches the Phase 21 `data-today-line-side='body|header'` precedent for the body+header symmetric pair.
- **`resolvedTodayCellBg`** (computed name): "resolved" prefix matches `resolvedTodayLine` (Phase 21) and `resolveBarStyle` (Phase 20).
- **`TODAY_CELL_BODY` + `TODAY_CELL_HEADER`** (reference-DOM-map constants): two separate exports because k-ui uses two different class names for the two sides. Same shape as Phase 22's `TOOLBAR_ROOT` / `TOOLBAR_TITLE` family.

### Open / parked (Phase 22.2)

- **Per-view today-bg-color override** — k-ui doesn't expose; just one global token. Per-view override is in the `views: {}` cluster (Defer-indefinite per PARITY_RECHECK).
- **`.gantt-day-today` (month-view path)** — not exercised by chronix gantt's six views. Stays in baseline as a Defer-indefinite class within the day-header customization cluster.
- **Live midnight rollover** — same parking as Phase 21 todayLine. `Date.now()` sampled at render time only.
- **Hourly granularity for today-cell** — chronix paints ONE rect spanning 24 hours; k-ui paints 24 separate rects. Both visually identical, but chronix's render is cheaper (1 SVG element vs 24×N). No follow-up; chronix's approach is intentional design.

## Phase 22.2 — DONE

- 3 commits: `59c34f3` (design doc, 169 lines) + `8d92b79` (Commit 1: core + adapter + 6 SFC tests, 228 lines) + `ffdb965` (Commit 2: demo + parity assertion + 15 VRT re-baselines + audit corrections, 134 LOC + 15 PNGs).
- **267/267 core vitest** unchanged. **211/211 vue3 adapter** (+6 todayCellBg SFC). **11/11 demo vitest** unchanged. **Cumulative vitest 483 → 489**.
- **golden-runner Playwright unit tests 32 unchanged**.
- **31 → 32 parity assertions** (+1 todayCellBg x+w). **Day-1 result: kui x=2496 w=1248 chronix x=2496 w=1248 Δx=Δw=0.00 — pixel-perfect**.
- **27 cross-demo scenarios** (12 cross + 15 vrt). Gate: 27/27 green after 15 chronix-self VRT re-baselines.
- **5 chronix VRT + 6 k-ui parity goldens + 17 chronix-visual baselines** unchanged.
- **KUI_SURFACE_BASELINE**: 359 → 361 items (audit-sweep class-attribution correction). Catalog-completeness scan clean.
- `/phase-close` skill walked all 7 gates green (6 standard + 6.5 cross-demo-verify).
- ci-check fully green.
- **Side outcome**: corrected the audit-sweep's `.gantt-day-today` mis-attribution in PARITY_RECHECK + added the correct classes to baseline. Demonstrates the silent-gap audit can have its own bugs that surface when classes are actually tested against live demos — Phase 22.AUTOMATE's gate caught nothing here because the WRONG class WAS dispositioned; the runtime parity assertion caught it. The two gates are complementary: catalog-completeness catches missing dispositions; live parity catches incorrect ones.

## Phase 24 — Imperative handle API + nav (DONE, 2026-05-16)

First chronix release that exposes a real `GanttHandle` via the Vue3 adapter's `expose()`. 11 nav/scroll/lookup methods land per design doc, plus 4 pre-existing typed-only data accessors get their first real wiring (the design doc claimed Phase 4+ coverage but no adapter had ever instantiated them — Phase 24 closes that vapor-typed debt).

### Reference reading (Phase 24)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/api/GanttSchedulerImpl.ts:1-525` — full 33-method imperative surface; each method's call shape (Date vs DurationInput, optional viewType, etc.); cross-over policies on `changeView` (line 110-143) and `zoomTo` (line 148-168).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/api/GanttSchedulerImpl.ts:200-237` — `prev` / `next` / `today` / `prevYear` / `nextYear` all call `unselect()` then `dispatch({ type: 'CHANGE_DATE', dateMarker: ... })`. K-ui auto-clears selection on nav; chronix does not (selection is consumer-owned via `selectedBarIds` prop).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/api/GanttSchedulerImpl.ts:518-524` — `scrollToTime(timeInput: DurationInput)` triggers internal `_scrollRequest` event; k-ui's scroll happens asynchronously via reducer-driven scroll-restoration, NOT direct DOM mutation. Diverges from chronix's design which writes `wrapperRef.scrollLeft` synchronously.
- `audit/PHASE_22_TOOLBAR_DESIGN.md` — controlled-prop `update:axisInput` pathway: Phase 24 methods funnel through the same channel.
- `audit/SILENT_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md` Section D — 33-method enumeration with 5-way disposition, drove Phase 24's scope-B selection (11 methods).
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` Disposition register — `addEvent` / `removeAllEvents` originally bundled into Phase 24 scope; deferred to Phase 26+ to preserve single-session discipline (write CRUD needs transaction-overlay commit semantics + new emit events).

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 24)

- **Compute-and-emit pathway**: `handle.next()` reads `props.axisInput`, calls `nextAnchor(viewId, anchorDate)` from Phase 22's nav-utils, emits `update:axisInput` with the new shape. The consumer's `v-model:axis-input` round-trips, prop reactively updates, chart re-renders. Single source of truth — no internal-state hybrid. Same channel as toolbar widget clicks (Phase 22). Failure mode: consumer forgets to wire `v-model:axis-input` → emit fires-and-forgotten, chart stays put. Documented as the contract.
- **`scrollToDate` is the documented exception**: scroll position has never been a chronix prop, so it can't go through the controlled-prop pathway. Writes `wrapperRef.scrollLeft` directly. Computes x via the active axis: `axisStartMs = axis.ticks[0]?.time.getTime()` + `pxPerMs = slotWidth / slotDurationMs` (chronix's standard per-pass derivation; PlannedAxis doesn't pre-compute `pxPerMs`). Browser auto-clamps to `[0, scrollWidth - clientWidth]`.
- **`expose()` is the Vue3-native ref-exposure shape**: Vue 3 `defineComponent`'s `setup(props, { expose })` receives an `expose` callback as the 3rd destructured field. Calling `expose({ method, ... })` makes those keys appear on the component proxy at `wrapper.vm` in tests and `ref.value.method()` at the consumer site. Phase 24 builds the `handle: GanttHandle` object after all setup state (axis, wrapperRef, etc.) is in scope but before `return () => { ... }` — handle closures capture reactive sources directly.
- **`subscribe` registry via emit-tee**: every adapter `emit(name, payload)` callsite was wrapped in a new `emitToBoth(name, payload)` helper that ALSO notifies any registered listeners in a `Map<EventName, Set<Listener>>`. Returns an unsubscribe function. Required because Vue 3's emit isn't externally subscribable — `ref.value.subscribe(...)` needs a separate side-channel. ~14 emit callsites mechanically replaced.
- **`GanttEventMap` was incomplete**: Phase 4-era `GanttEventMap` had 7 event keys (bar-drop, bar-resize, progress-change, bar-click, select, view-change, bars-set) but the adapter emits 15 events; the toolbar's `update:axisInput` (Phase 22) and most lifecycle emits (bar-dragstart/-stop/-resizestart/etc) were never registered there. Phase 24 added the `update:axisInput` key (required for handle.subscribe to type-check against the methods Phase 24 ships); the rest of the lifecycle-event additions are out of scope but cataloged as a follow-up.
- **k-ui's `getApi().scrollToTime` is async**: k-ui's `scrollToTime(timeInput)` triggers an internal `_scrollRequest` event handled by a reducer that updates state, then a scroll-restoration mechanism scrolls the actual DOM element. Cross-demo parity for the SCROLL BEHAVIOR is therefore parked: chronix's contract is "write wrapper.scrollLeft synchronously", k-ui's contract is "dispatch scroll request and let the reducer settle it". User-visible outcome equivalent; internal mechanism diverges.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 24)

- `packages/gantt/src/api/gantt-handle.ts` (+70 LOC): extended `GanttHandle` interface with 11 new method signatures organized into View/nav (8 methods), Scroll (1 method), Read-only bar lookup (2 methods). New `IncrementDelta` interface (`{ days?, weeks?, months?, years? }`).
- `packages/gantt/src/api/nav-utils.ts` (+36 LOC): new `applyIncrement(anchor, delta)` helper using `Date.setFullYear / setMonth / setDate` in canonical order (years → months → weeks → days).
- `packages/gantt/src/api/gantt-options.ts` (+10 LOC): added `'update:axisInput': AxisRangePlanInput` to `GanttEventMap` (was missing since Phase 4/22 era).
- `packages/gantt/src/api/index.ts` + `packages/gantt/src/index.ts` (+2 LOC each): re-export `IncrementDelta` + `applyIncrement`.
- `packages/gantt/src/api/nav-utils.test.ts` (+72 LOC): 8 new tests for `applyIncrement` covering days/weeks/months/years/combinations/zero-delta/non-mutation.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (+210 LOC): `setup(props, { emit, expose })` builds `handle: GanttHandle` with 11 Phase-24 methods + 4 pre-existing typed-only data accessors implemented inline (`getBarTable` / `getRowDataSource` / `getLinkTable` as minimal reactive wrappers over props; `subscribe` as a `Map<key, Set<Listener>>` registry). New `emitToBoth(name, payload)` helper teed across all 14 adapter emit callsites. `expose(handle)` makes everything accessible.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-handle.test.ts` (NEW, 223 LOC): 18 SFC tests via `mount(ChronixGantt)` + `wrapper.vm as unknown as GanttHandle`. Covers each nav method's emit shape (`update:axisInput` payload), `getDate()` prop-reactivity (`wrapper.setProps({...})` → handle.getDate() reflects), `scrollToDate` DOM write (asserts numeric `wrapperEl.scrollLeft`), read-only lookups, data-accessor shapes (BarTable/RowDataSource/LinkTable), subscribe lifecycle (fires alongside emit; unsubscribes correctly).
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue` (+30 LOC): new `ganttRef = ref<GanttHandle | null>(null)` + 4 demo test-buttons at `data-test-handle-method='next|today|changeView-month|scrollToDate'` driving `ganttRef?.next()` etc. New `scrollTargetDate()` helper returns `anchorDate + 1 day` for deterministic scroll target.
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/styles.css` (+15 LOC): `.cx-demo-handle-test-bar` positioned `top:-9999px; left:-9999px; width:1px; height:1px; overflow:hidden` — clickable by Playwright but invisible to humans / VRT snapshots.
- Reference-side `d:/work/k-ui/examples/gantt/vue3/src/DemoApp.vue` (+50 LOC, separate k-ui-repo edits): matching test-button bar + 4 handler functions invoking the equivalent imperative methods. Not committed to the k-ui repo as part of Phase 24; user owns those commits.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+200 LOC): 4 new cross-demo parity assertions — `phase24-handle.next` (toolbar title shift on both sides), `phase24-handle.changeView(month)` (pressed-state on both sides), `phase24-handle.today` (title contains current year on both sides), `phase24-handle.scrollToDate` (chronix-only: `cx-gantt-wrapper.scrollLeft > 0`; reference-side scroll mechanism is async + uses different element, cross-demo parity for behavior parked).
- 5 chronix-visual VRT baselines re-captured (1-px wrapper-height shift from Phase 24's offscreen test-button bar; same architectural pattern as Phase 22's `.cx-gantt-root` introduction).

**Test count after Phase 24**:

- vitest: 489 → **515** (+26). Core: 267 → 275 (+8 applyIncrement). Adapter: 211 → 229 (+18 chronix-gantt-handle SFC). Demo: 11 unchanged.
- golden-runner Playwright unit tests: 32 unchanged.
- parity.spec.ts: 32 → **36** assertions (+4 phase24-handle.\* ).
