## Phase 28.3 — barClassNames + onLine + useLineEventColor + link slot (DONE, 2026-05-17)

Closes the cluster C remainder from `audit/RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md` after Phase 28.2 (font cascade) shipped — 4 additive customization surfaces consumers were missing: `barClassNamesCallback` (per-bar CSS classes), `onLineCallback` (per-link marker / color override), `useLineEventColor` (line stroke inherits source-bar color), and a `'link'` slot in the slot registry (full link-render replacement). User-approved scope **A** (full bundle — all 4 surfaces) / **A** (`onLineCallback` render-time scope only — no routing-type mutation) / **A** (`barClassNamesCallback` applies to main `.cx-gantt-bar` rect only — Phase 28.1 selection-border / resize-zone / dot rects keep stable themed selectors).

### Reference reading (Phase 28.3)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/common/EventContainer.tsx:120-131` — `classNameGenerator={options.eventClassNames}` resolves classes per event via `ContentContainer`. Generator type: `ClassNamesGenerator<EventContentArg>` (returns `string | string[] | undefined`).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/DependencyLineAlgorithm.ts:60-95` — `DependencyLine` shape + `OnLineCallback = (line: DependencyLine) => DependencyLine | void`. Mutable fields: `type`, `markerType`, `customMarker`, `extraVerticalOffset`, `forceVerticalDown`.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineDependencies.tsx:33-35` — `onLine` accepts single OR array form; `useLineEventColor` boolean enables source-bar color inheritance.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineDependencies.tsx:1038-1062` — callbacks registered via `algorithm.registerOnLine(cb)`, walked in registration order.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineDependencies.tsx:2337-2339` + `2670-2693` — `useLineEventColor` resolution at color-collection time so marker defs include the right color.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 28.3)

- **`barClassNamesCallback` cascade slot**: piggybacks on Phase 20's `BarStyleArg` cascade. Resolver runs the class callback in the same Layer-4 block as color + font callbacks; the `BarStyleArg` it receives carries the cascaded color / font defaults from layers 1-3 so the callback can branch on resolved bg / fg if it wants. Returns `string | readonly string[] | undefined`; resolver normalizes to `readonly string[]` on `ResolvedBarStyle.classNames` (string → single-entry; undefined → empty).
- **Class scope = main `.cx-gantt-bar` rect only** (chronix divergence from k-ui's group-class wrapping): chronix's flat per-bar render emits selection-border / resize-zone / dot rects as siblings with their own `cx-gantt-bar-*` modifier classes. Consumer CSS targets the main rect via class composition (`.priority-high.cx-gantt-bar { ... }`); Phase 28.1 visuals stay theme-controlled and unaffected by consumer classes. Avoids a structural change (no per-bar `<g>` wrapper) that would have broken adapter tests + cross-demo VRT.
- **`onLineCallback` render-time scope (v0)**: callback fires in the adapter AFTER `LinkRouter` completes. Returns `{ color?, marker? }` — replaces those channels only. Routing-type mutation (`'square'` ↔ `'smooth'`) is NOT supported because it would require re-running LinkRouter; deferred to Phase 28.3.1 if a consumer asks. The parity reference's most common host use of `onLine` is color + markerType swapping (highlight critical paths, switch arrow → diamond for warnings); the routing-type mutation is uncommon.
- **`useLineEventColor` cascade**: `colorOverride > useLineEventColor source-bar-bg > theme.linkDefaultColor`. Resolved at adapter render-time using a per-render `barColorByBarId` map populated during the per-bar flatMap. Source bar's resolved background color (Phase 20 cascade output) becomes the link stroke when the toggle is true and no overrides apply.
- **Marker defs collection uses post-callback resolved colors + customMarkers**: a key insight from the k-ui reference. If `onLineCallback` returns a new color for a link, the adapter must emit a `<marker>` def at that color so the link's `marker-end="url(#cx-marker-...)"` reference resolves. Same for callback-returned custom markers — they may not be in `props.links` but still need defs. Achieved by building a `resolvedLinks` array in one pass, then keying defs off the post-callback shapes.
- **`'link'` slot mirrors Phase 11's `'bar'` slot**: consumer template fully replaces the default `<path class="cx-gantt-link">` per routed link. Args carry pre-resolved color + marker (after `useLineEventColor` + `onLineCallback`), so a template that just wants chronix defaults can drop them straight into its own `<path>`. Slot template return is the framework's VNode shape (Vue3: `VNode | VNode[] | null`); adapter normalizes null → empty for null-skip behavior.
- **One callback per chart vs k-ui's array form**: chronix v0 accepts a single `onLineCallback` function; consumers chaining rules call multiple helpers inside one function. K-ui accepts `OnLineCallback | OnLineCallback[]` for composing host-side rules — defer-indefinite for chronix until a consumer asks. Same precedent as Phase 20's color callbacks (single function per channel).

One existing `toEqual` assertion extended with `classNames: []`.

Marker `<defs>` collection now uses post-callback resolved colors AND post-callback `CustomLinkMarker` overrides.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-bar-classnames.test.ts` (new, ~120 LOC, +6 tests).

- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue` (+~3 LOC): `useLineEventColor` toggle in `DEMO_SCHEMA` + binding on `<ChronixGantt>`.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+~35 LOC): architectural-divergence note documenting why no cross-demo parity assertions land for Phase 28.3 (chronix-additive callbacks + missing parity-mode links).

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 28.3)

- **`vi.fn(() => 'x')` inferred empty-tuple parameter list** (typecheck finding): the mock test for "class callback receives the same `BarStyleArg`" used `const seen = vi.fn(() => 'x')`; TS inferred `Parameters<typeof seen>` as `[]` (empty tuple), so `seen.mock.calls[0]![0]` errored with "Tuple type '[]' of length '0' has no element at index '0'". Fix: explicitly type the mock implementation: `const seen = vi.fn((_arg: BarStyleArg): string => 'x')`. Lesson echoing past TS-strict findings: `vi.fn` with an inline implementation infers from the implementation's signature, not the call-site usage; give it an explicit type when the test later reads `mock.calls`.
- **Existing `toEqual({...})` ResolvedBarStyle shape break**: the new `classNames` field on `ResolvedBarStyle` broke one existing test that asserted the full shape. Caught at first test run after Commit 2. Single update + ci-check green. Pattern: adding required fields to exact-shape return types ripples to every `toEqual` consumer; consider `.toMatchObject` for tests focused on subset semantics, or update + accept the ripple. Updated `toEqual` was cheaper this time (1 consumer).
- **Parity fixture has no links → cross-demo `useLineEventColor` infeasible**: discovered when checking the chronix parity-mode demo's wiring (`initialLinks = cfg.parity.value ? [] : sampleLinks`). The parity-events fixture mirrors only event geometry, not the k-ui demo's 33 dependency entries. Mirroring them would be a separate fixture-design task (event ids + dependency directions verbatim from upstream). Decision: drop both planned `useLineEventColor` parity assertions; document architectural divergence; rely on 9 adapter tests. Same pattern as Phase 28.1's selection-state deferral.

### Naming justifications (Phase 28.3)

- **`barClassNamesCallback`** (component prop, vs `barClassNames` / `eventClassNamesCallback`): `bar` prefix matches chronix's existing `barColor` / `barBackgroundColorCallback` convention; `ClassNames` is the parity-reference's term verbatim; `Callback` suffix mirrors Phase 20's 3 color callbacks + Phase 28.2's font callbacks. Rejected `barClassNames` (no `Callback` suffix) because it could read as a static array prop — the suffix disambiguates.
- **`BarClassNamesFunc`** (callback type, vs `BarClassNamesGenerator`): parallels `BarColorFunc` / `BarFontSizeFunc` / `BarFontWeightFunc`. K-ui's `ClassNamesGenerator` is a generic over `RenderProps`; chronix's flat callback shape doesn't need the generic.
- **`LinkRenderFunc` / `LinkRenderArg` / `LinkRenderOverride`** (callback types, vs `OnLineCallback` / `DependencyLine` k-ui names): `Link` prefix matches chronix's `LinkSpec` / `LinkRouter` terminology (chronix uses "link", k-ui uses "dependency line"). `RenderArg` + `RenderOverride` split the input (chronix-named arg bag) from the output (chronix-named partial override) — k-ui's single `DependencyLine` shape serves both roles; chronix keeps them separate for clearer API contracts.
- **`onLineCallback`** (component prop, vs `onLine` / `lineCallback`): `on` prefix matches the parity-reference's `onLine` term + signals "fires per element" (parallel to `onSelect` / `onBarDrop` emit handlers chronix already has). The `Callback` suffix again disambiguates from a potential `onLine` data prop. Long-form intentional — chronix consumers see the prop name typed at every binding site, so explicit > terse.
- **`useLineEventColor`** (component prop, kept verbatim from k-ui): no chronix alternative reads better; the name describes the behavior (use the source event's color for the line). Boolean default `false` so existing consumers see no change.
- **`LINK_SLOT_NAME`** (vs `LINK_SLOT_ID` / `'link'` literal): mirrors the existing `BAR_SLOT_NAME` from Phase 11. Consumer code reads `registry.register(LINK_SLOT_NAME, ...)` for symbolic clarity; chronix can rename the literal later without breaking caller code.
- **`barColorByBarId`** (file-private adapter Map, vs `placedBarColors` / `resolvedBgByBarId`): emphasizes the key (`barId`) and the value type (`Color`, i.e. `string`); the `By` connector is a chronix-native convention used elsewhere (`overlayIdByBarId`, `barProgressById`). Disambiguates from the Phase 12 `selectedBarSet` (different shape, different lookup semantics).
- **`resolvedLinks` (interface `ResolvedLinkRender`)** (in-loop temporary structure, vs `LinkRenderCtx` / `LinkRenderInfo`): the name describes "what the render block resolved per link before emitting" — color + marker + bars. The interface lives at function scope to keep adapter-internal vs public-API types separate.

### Open / parked (Phase 28.3)

- **`onLineCallback` routing-type mutation (`routing: 'square' | 'smooth'`)** — defer-indefinite. Would require re-running LinkRouter on callback output; impacts the layout-pass purity. Reprioritize when a consumer asks for dynamic routing-style switching per link. K-ui's `DependencyLine.type` mutation covers this case in the parity reference.
- **`onLineCallback` array form (`OnLineCallback | OnLineCallback[]`)** — defer-indefinite. Single function per chart suffices for v0; consumers chaining rules call helpers inside one function. Same precedent as Phase 20 color callbacks.
- **`onLineCallback` `extraVerticalOffset` override** — defer-indefinite. Chronix's LinkRouter doesn't expose per-link vertical-offset surface (v0 routes by bar bounds only). Reprioritize when LinkRouter grows offset support OR a consumer asks for vertical-routing customization.
- **`onLineCallback` `forceVerticalDown` flag** — defer-indefinite. Chronix's LinkRouter v0 path is always "right-of-source / left-of-target"; no vertical-first detour direction to control. Reprioritize when chronix routing grows complex enough to need direction flags.
- **`barResizerDotBorderWidth` separate token** — already deferred from Phase 28.1; chronix v0 hard-codes border width to 1 px. Reprioritize when a consumer asks for thick-bordered dots.
- **Cross-demo `useLineEventColor` parity (2 assertions originally planned)** — defer to Phase 28.3.1. Requires extending `buildParityEvents` with dependency arrays mirroring the parity reference's 33 dependency entries + threading `sampleLinksParity` through the chronix demo's parity mode. With both sides carrying links, the 2 assertions (link-color set parity + marker-def color set parity) become straightforward.
- **Cross-demo `barClassNamesCallback` / `onLineCallback` / link slot parity** — defer-indefinite. The 3 surfaces are chronix-additive consumer hooks; the parity reference's demo doesn't wire equivalents (its `eventClassNames` and `onLine` defaults are no-ops in the default `DemoApp.vue` setup). Cross-demo testing would require modifying both demos, which isn't a parity-oracle concern.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 28.3)

Design-doc estimate: 7h, ~1090 LOC + 0-2 PNGs. Actual:

- Commit 1 (`de33a37`) design: 677 LOC (over estimate ~600; prettier reformatted the wide disposition table — same pattern as Phase 26 / 27 / 28.1 / 28.2).
- Commit 2 (`c883ebd`) core: 436 LOC across 9 files (3 new src + 3 new test + 3 index updates). On budget.

- Commit 5 (wrap-up): this commit.
- **Total**: ~1900 LOC across 4 commits in ~5 hours (under 7h estimate). Zero VRT churn — third consecutive "no re-baseline needed" phase (Phase 27 + Phase 28.1 also zero). Pattern: render-layer additions that are conditional (callback set / toggle on / slot registered) produce no VRT cost because the default demo state doesn't exercise them.

**Verdict**: single-session discipline held. The mid-phase finding (parity fixture has no links → cross-demo `useLineEventColor` infeasible) demonstrated the same pattern as Phase 28.1's selection-state deferral: discovering at parity-test-design time that the parity oracle's setup is incompatible with the test's premise. Resolved by documenting the divergence + relying on adapter unit tests for the load-bearing coverage. The `feedback_chronix_parity_discipline.md` mandate handles this gracefully: cross-demo parity is mandatory IF FEASIBLE; when infeasibility is structurally documented, the discipline accepts adapter tests as the substitute. Cluster C of the 2026-05-16 RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP is now fully closed.

## Phase 29 — per-day/per-slot CSS classes + header cell slot/callback (DONE, 2026-05-17)

Closes Cluster D from `audit/RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP_2026-05-16.md` (Sections I + N.1 + N.2). Four chronix-additive surfaces: body slot rects with `cx-gantt-slot` + `cx-gantt-slot-{dayId}` + state classes; header day cells (week/day views) and tick row labels (month/season/halfYear/year views) gain `cx-gantt-day` + `cx-gantt-day-{dayId}` + state classes; new `headerCellClassNamesCallback` prop for per-cell consumer classes; new `HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME = 'header-cell'` slot for full header cell render replacement. User-approved scope **A** (full bundle in one phase) / **A** (mirror k-ui day/slot taxonomy split, REJECT `-other` as architectural divergence, PARK `-disabled`) / **A** (BOTH callback AND slot — mirrors Phase 28.3 bar / link pattern).

### Reference reading (Phase 29)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/component/date-rendering.ts:1-81` — `DateMeta` + `getDayClassNames(meta, theme)` + `getSlotClassNames(meta, theme)` helpers. Day family includes `-other`; slot family omits it. Both index dayId via Sun-anchored `DAY_IDS`.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/common/TableDateCell.tsx:29-89` — header cell render in CALENDAR-grid views: `getDayClassNames` applied at `elClasses` + `dayHeaderFormat` / `dayHeaderContent` / `dayHeaderClassNames` / `dayHeaderDidMount` callback surface.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/common/DayCellContainer.tsx:1-66` — body cell render in calendar views.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/datelib/marker.ts` — `DAY_IDS` literal (Sun-anchored, 7 entries).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:481-616` — the resource-timeline view's `renderTimelineHeader`. **CRITICAL FINDING**: this path NEVER calls `getDayClassNames`. The day-class taxonomy in the parity reference is calendar-grid-only; the resource-timeline (chronix's mirror surface) renders header cells through a hardcoded `<text>` path that emits only `gantt-timeline-header-cell` + Phase 22.2's today-cell rect.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 29)

- **No PlannedAxis shape extension** (load-bearing simplification): all day / slot meta derives at render time from existing `tick.time` + a fresh `startOfDay(new Date())` reference. Zero fixture-test churn — contrast with Phase 27's `PlacedBar.isStart`/`isEnd` additions that rippled through 6 fixture files. This was the key cost-saver vs the original 8-10h scope estimate.
- **Day class eligibility split**:
  - **Outer band cells**: eligible when `(cell.width / slotWidth) × slotDurationMs === MS_PER_DAY` (floating-point tolerant). Day view's single anchor cell + week view's 7 day cells pass; month/season/halfYear/year month-bands fail (multi-day spans).
  - **Tick row labels**: eligible when `slotDurationMs >= MS_PER_DAY` (i.e. one tick = one day). Month/season/halfYear/year pass; day/week (hourly) fail.
  - When eligible, the cell gets `getDayClassNames(dayMeta)` appended. When ineligible, the cell still gets the callback (which can use `date` or `label` for other branching) but no day classes.
- **Body slot rects (chronix-additive)**: emitted as one transparent `<rect class="cx-gantt-slot ...">` per axis tick in a new `<g class="cx-gantt-slots">` group. Layered BEHIND grid lines (so grid strokes paint over them) + behind bars / links (so consumer fills don't obscure chrome). `pointer-events: none` so they don't intercept any pointer interaction. `fill: transparent` so default render stays pixel-identical to pre-Phase-29.
- **`HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME = 'header-cell'`**: parallels `BAR_SLOT_NAME` (Phase 11) and `LINK_SLOT_NAME` (Phase 28.3). Consulted via the existing `slotRegistry` prop — no new prop needed. When registered, template fires per header cell (outer band cells AND tick row labels); return value replaces the default `<rect>+<text>` pair (outer band) or `<text>` label (tick row, where the boundary `<line>` is structural and stays). Args include `bandIndex` (0 = tick row, 1+ = outer bands), pre-resolved `dayMeta`, and `extraClasses` populated by any callback output so slot consumers can compose the callback's contribution.
- **`headerCellClassNamesCallback`**: returns `string | readonly string[] | undefined`; classes append to the primary cell element (outer band `<rect>` or tick row `<text>`). Same return-normalization pattern as `barClassNamesCallback` (Phase 28.3). Fires for ALL header cells (outer + tick) so consumers can branch on `bandIndex` if they need different rules per row.
- **`-other` architectural rejection (chronix-divergent)**: chronix's month view is a continuous timeline of in-range days (30 daily slots), not a 7×6 calendar grid with prev/next-month padding days. So `gantt-day-other`'s semantic doesn't apply on the chronix side. Documented in design doc + asserted via a sweep-all-6-views adapter test that never finds `-other` on any rendered cell.
- **`-disabled` parked**: chronix's PlannedAxis has no `validRange` / `activeRange` concept (k-ui's DateProfile carries those). All chronix days are "active" in v0. Class never emitted. Re-prioritize when `disabledDateRange` prop lands (likely Phase 31+).

### Chronix work derived (Phase 29)

- `packages/gantt/src/render/cell-state-classes.ts` (new, ~85 LOC): `DAY_IDS` (Sun-anchored 7-element literal), `DayId`, `CellStateMeta`, `computeCellStateMeta(date, today)`, `getDayClassNames(meta)`, `getSlotClassNames(meta)`. Pure functions; no allocations beyond the returned `string[]`.
- `packages/gantt/src/render/cell-state-classes.test.ts` (new, ~145 LOC, +12 tests): DAY_IDS order matches k-ui verbatim; getDay() indexing; computeCellStateMeta dayId / isToday / isPast / isFuture across boundary cases; day/slot class output minimum sets + state modifier appends; `-other` never emitted on either family (architectural rejection guard).
- `packages/gantt/src/render/header-cell-slot.ts` (new, ~60 LOC): `HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME = 'header-cell'` + `HeaderCellSlotArgs` interface (bandIndex / cellIndex / geometry / label / date / dayMeta / theme / optional cell or tick / optional extraClasses).
- `packages/gantt/src/render/header-cell-slot.test.ts` (new, ~85 LOC, +4 tests): constant value; args shape for both band-cell and tick-row invocations; slot registry round-trip.
- `packages/gantt/src/render/index.ts` + `packages/gantt/src/index.ts`: 5 new public-API re-exports (`DAY_IDS`, `DayId`, `CellStateMeta`, `computeCellStateMeta`, `getDayClassNames`, `getSlotClassNames`, `HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME`, `HeaderCellSlotArgs`).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (+~210 LOC):
  - New types `HeaderCellArg` + `HeaderCellClassNamesFunc` (adapter-local since they're chronix-specific render-time shapes; the callback isn't part of any core cascade like `BarClassNamesFunc` is).
  - New prop `headerCellClassNamesCallback`.
  - `deriveBandCellMeta(cell)` derives date + dayMeta from cell x / width geometry vs axis start time and slot duration. Tolerance check for one-day eligibility.
  - `deriveTickMeta(tick)` derives dayMeta for day-resolution views only.
  - `callHeaderCellClassNames(arg)` normalizes the callback's return into `readonly string[]`.
  - Header band cell loop rewritten: invokes callback + reads slot template + falls through to default `<rect>+<text>` with day classes appended when eligible.
  - Tick row loop rewritten: structural `<line>` separator always renders; label `<text>` (or slot template's return) renders next with day classes appended when day-resolution.
  - Body SVG `bodySlotChildren` block: one transparent `<rect>` per axis tick inside a `<g class="cx-gantt-slots">` group, layered between today-cell-bg and grid-vlines.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-slot-classes.test.ts` (new, ~140 LOC, +6 tests): body slot rect count per view; day-id assignment; week view Sat/Sun counts; today/past/future counts in week view; rect geometry (width / height / y); month view per-day classes.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-day-classes.test.ts` (new, ~130 LOC, +5 tests): week view 7 day cells with weekday classes; today's day cell carries `-today`; month view tick labels carry day + state classes; day view's single outer cell; `-other` never emitted across all 6 views.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-header-cell-callback.test.ts` (new, ~125 LOC, +5 tests): no callback → no extras; array return; string return; undefined return; HeaderCellArg shape verification (bandIndex / cellIndex / date / dayMeta correctness).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-header-cell-slot.test.ts` (new, ~130 LOC, +4 tests): no slot → defaults; slot replaces both band cells AND tick labels; slot args geometry + dayMeta; `extraClasses` surfaces callback output.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+~35 LOC): architectural-divergence note documenting why no cross-demo parity assertions land for Phase 29 (parity reference's `getDayClassNames` is calendar-view-only; resource-timeline view chronix mirrors never invokes it; chronix's adoption IS the additive surface).
- **VRT impact**: zero re-baseline. 27/27 cross-demo verify green; 5/5 chronix-visual baselines unchanged. Class-only additions with no inline color have zero default-state pixel impact. Fourth consecutive 0-VRT phase (Phase 27 / 28.1 / 28.3 / 29).

**Test count after Phase 29**:

- vitest: 614 → **651** (+37). Core: 313 → 329 (+16: 12 cell-state-classes + 4 header-cell-slot). Adapter: 291 → 311 (+20: 6 slot-classes + 5 day-classes + 5 header-cell-callback + 4 header-cell-slot). Demo: 11 unchanged. Slightly over the +33 design estimate due to expanded coverage in `cell-state-classes.test.ts` (DAY_IDS indexing + boundary cases for isToday).

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 29)

- **Parity-plan infeasibility discovered at Commit 4**: design doc proposed `phase29-day-today class presence parity (week view)` + `phase29-day-id class set parity` assertions, both querying `.gantt-day-today` / `.gantt-day-{dayId}` on the parity reference's DOM. Grep of `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/` for `getDayClassNames` returned no matches — confirming the helper is calendar-view-only, never invoked in the resource-timeline view chronix mirrors. So those classes never appear in the parity-reference demo's DOM in any view chronix exercises. Decision: drop both assertions; declare chronix-new with rationale; pin the cross-CSS-portability invariant (chronix class names match k-ui's DAY_IDS order verbatim) via the core unit test. Third consecutive phase with this pattern (Phase 28.1 selection-state, Phase 28.3 useLineEventColor, Phase 29 day classes) — the discipline's mandate ("cross-demo parity IF FEASIBLE, otherwise document the divergence") absorbs it gracefully.
- **Cluster D scope eligibility math edge case**: deriving "cell represents one day" from `(cell.width / slotWidth) × slotDurationMs === MS_PER_DAY` needed floating-point tolerance. The slotWidth derivation in `axisRangePlanner` uses `Math.max(stretched, floor)` so `cellSpanMs` can land at `86399999.something` for some viewport widths. Used `Math.abs(cellSpanMs - MS_PER_DAY) < 1` (1 ms tolerance) — generous enough that any floating drift inside a single render passes, tight enough that no multi-day cell accidentally qualifies.
- **No PlannedAxis extension intentional simplification paid off**: zero fixture-test churn (vs Phase 27's 6 file ripple). Time saved went into expanded test coverage (+4 over estimate).
- **Adapter import-order lint warnings (2 fix-ups)**: my new `header-cell-slot.test.ts` triggered `import-x/order` warnings (k-ui type imports interleaved with internal imports). Same pattern as link-slot.test.ts pre-existing warnings — adapter ESLint config strictly requires external imports first, then internal, with blank line separators. Quick reorder fix.

### Naming justifications (Phase 29)

- **`cx-gantt-day-*` / `cx-gantt-slot-*`** (vs unified `cx-gantt-cell-*` or slot-only): mirror the parity reference's class taxonomy 1:1 with the chronix `cx-` prefix. Consumers porting CSS from k-ui calendar views (`.gantt-day-sat`, `.gantt-day-today`) map by find-replace to `.cx-gantt-day-sat` / `.cx-gantt-day-today` etc. Unified `cx-gantt-cell-*` would have lost the portability hook; slot-only would have lost the day-cell-state hook on header bands.
- **`DAY_IDS`** (vs `WEEKDAY_IDS` / `DOW_IDS`): verbatim from the parity reference (k-ui's `datelib/marker.ts`). Keeps consumer expectations stable.
- **`HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME = 'header-cell'`** (vs `'headerCell'` camelCase or `HEADER_CELL_SLOT_ID`): kebab-case literal matches Phase 11's `'bar'` + Phase 28.3's `'link'` pattern. `_NAME` suffix matches the existing slot constants.
- **`HeaderCellSlotArgs`** (vs `HeaderCellRenderArg` / `HeaderCellSlotCtx`): `SlotArgs` suffix mirrors `BarSlotArgs` (Phase 11) + `LinkSlotArgs` (Phase 28.3). Consistency across the 3 slots.
- **`headerCellClassNamesCallback`** (vs `headerCellClasses` / `headerCellClassCallback`): `ClassNames` (plural) matches the parity reference's `dayHeaderClassNames` term + Phase 28.3's `barClassNamesCallback`. `Callback` suffix disambiguates from a potential `headerCellClasses` static prop.
- **`HeaderCellArg`** (vs `HeaderCellRenderArg` / `HeaderCellClassArg`): parallels `BarStyleArg` (Phase 20 + 28.2 + 28.3) and `LinkRenderArg` (Phase 28.3). Single-word `Arg` suffix kept terse.
- **`computeCellStateMeta`** (vs `deriveCellStateMeta` / `getCellStateMeta` / `cellStateMetaFor`): `compute` connotes pure-function derivation (vs `derive` which can read more procedural). Matches `computeRowSpans` (existing adapter helper).
- **`bodySlotChildren` + `<g class="cx-gantt-slots">`** (vs `bodySlotRects` / `<g class="cx-gantt-body-slots">`): the children are `<rect>` elements but the variable name shouldn't constrain that — if Phase 30+ adds slot-aware extras, they go in the same group. The group class drops `body-` because it's the only slot grouping (header tick row doesn't wrap its slot rects).

### Open / parked (Phase 29)

- **`cx-gantt-day-disabled` + `cx-gantt-slot-disabled` modifiers** — parked. Chronix's PlannedAxis has no `validRange` / `activeRange` analog of k-ui's DateProfile. Re-prioritize when chronix grows a `disabledDateRange` prop (likely Phase 31+ when input-validation surfaces land).
- **`cx-gantt-day-other` (out-of-current-month padding day)** — REJECTED as architectural divergence. chronix month view is a continuous timeline of in-range days; not a 7×6 calendar grid. The semantic doesn't apply. Documented in design doc + asserted by adapter sweep test.
- **`dayHeaderFormat` (label formatter per cell)** — REJECTED for Phase 29 scope. chronix's label formatting goes through `AxisRangePlanner` (`Intl.DateTimeFormat` configured per view). Per-cell label override needs a different abstraction (formatter chain on PlannedAxis input). Consumers wanting custom labels register the header-cell slot template instead (full replace covers it).
- **`dayHeaderContent` (callback returning content)** — parked. Overlaps strongly with the slot route (both replace cell content). Single replace-content API per phase keeps the surface clean; if consumer demand for "callback returning a string" emerges, re-prioritize as a thin wrapper that registers internally.
- **`dayHeaderDidMount` / `WillUnmount` lifecycle hooks** — parked. chronix has no equivalent for bar / link surfaces either. Defer until a coherent lifecycle-hook story for ALL render surfaces lands (Phase 31+).
- **Truncation tooltip via child `<title>`** — parked (chronix doesn't truncate header labels today; adding `<title>` is contingent on truncation landing first).
- **Theme tokens for day-state default colors (`dayTodayBg`, `daySatBg`, ...)** — REJECTED for v0. Per the design's load-bearing decision: classes-only emission keeps VRT at 0 PNG churn. Consumer CSS handles defaults. If consumer demand emerges for "chronix-default weekend tinting", re-prioritize as Phase 29.1.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 29)

Design-doc estimate: 7h, ~1070 LOC + 0 PNGs. Actual:

- Commit 1 (`6c155d8`) design: 599 LOC (close to ~600 estimate; prettier reformatted the wide disposition tables — same pattern as every prior Cluster phase).
- Commit 2 (`0c2875b`) core: 417 LOC across 6 files (2 new src + 2 new test + 2 index updates). Close to ~400 estimate. +16 vitest tests (4 over the +13 plan because of expanded boundary-case coverage in `cell-state-classes.test.ts`).
- Commit 3 (`7541c82`) adapter: 781 LOC across 5 files (1 src + 4 new test). On budget (~780).
- Commit 4 (`3a49c45`) parity divergence: 54 LOC across 2 files. Way under estimate (~100) because the 2 planned parity assertions were dropped — the work collapsed to an architectural-divergence note in parity.spec.ts + an "Implementation note" callout on the design doc.
- Commit 5 (wrap-up): this commit.
- **Total**: ~1850 LOC across 4 commits in ~5 hours (well under 7h estimate). Zero VRT churn — fourth consecutive "no re-baseline needed" phase (Phase 27 / 28.1 / 28.3 / 29). Pattern continues: class-only / conditional-emission additions produce no VRT cost because the default demo state doesn't exercise them visibly.

**Verdict**: single-session discipline held. Two key choices paid off: (1) **no PlannedAxis shape extension** (meta computed render-time from existing tick.time) avoided the 6-fixture-file ripple Phase 27 hit; (2) **class-only emission with no inline color** kept VRT at 0 PNG. The mid-phase finding (parity reference's `getDayClassNames` is calendar-view-only, not invoked in resource-timeline) was the third consecutive phase to discover at parity-test-design time that the parity oracle's setup is incompatible with the planned cross-demo assertions. The discipline's "chronix-new with rationale" escape hatch absorbed it cleanly; adapter unit tests + core helper test (verbatim DAY_IDS match) cover the load-bearing invariants. **Cluster D of the 2026-05-16 RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP is now fully closed.** Combined with Cluster A (Phase 26 grid lines), Cluster B (Phase 27 continuation triangles), and Cluster C (Phase 28.x bar render polish + customization), the post-sweep silent-gap remediation arc started at Phase 26 is now complete across all four clusters.

- `/phase-close` skill walked all 6 standard gates green.

- **Cluster D of the 2026-05-16 RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP fully closed**. chronix now ships: per-tick body slot rects with `cx-gantt-slot` + dayId + state classes (CSS hook for weekend tinting / today emphasis / past-future fade); per-header-day-cell `cx-gantt-day` + dayId + state classes (week / day views' outer band; month / season / halfYear / year tick row); `headerCellClassNamesCallback` for per-cell consumer classes; `HEADER_CELL_SLOT_NAME = 'header-cell'` for full cell render replacement. **Post-sweep silent-gap remediation arc COMPLETE across Clusters A/B/C/D** (Phases 26/27/28.1+28.2+28.3/29).

## Phase 23 — sidebar dual-scrollport architecture (DONE, 2026-05-17)

Closes the wrapper one-scroll-vs-two-scroll architectural divergence tracked at `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md:367` since the Phase 21 era (allocated 2026-05-16). Replaces chronix's single `<div class="cx-gantt-wrapper" overflow:auto>` + sticky-positioned panes model with two independent `overflow: auto` scroll containers (`cx-gantt-sidebar-pane` + `cx-gantt-chart-pane`), bidirectional vertical scroll-sync, and `transform: translateX`-driven horizontal header sync — matching the parity reference's `gantt-timeline-body-left` / `gantt-timeline-body-right` + `scrollingPaneRef` idiom verbatim. User-approved scope **A** (full bundle) / **A** (bidirectional sync with rAF-reset guard) / **A** (header siblings above panes with translateX) / **A** (clean replacement, accept 20-PNG VRT re-baseline, no `dualScrollport` flag-gate).

### Reference reading (Phase 23)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineLayout.tsx:74-185` — layout shell: CSS grid with `gantt-timeline-body-left` (sidebar pane, `overflow: auto`) + `gantt-timeline-body-right` (chart pane, `overflow: auto`) as siblings under a single grid row. Header pane sits above with `overflow: hidden` + tracks `scrollLeft` via `transform: translateX`.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineLayout.tsx:240-302` — `handleBodyLeftScroll` + `handleBodyRightScroll` — bidirectional vertical sync with `scrollingPaneRef` guard flag preventing the writeback loop. Source pane sets the ref; target pane reads + bails if mismatched. rAF reset clears the flag after the browser settles both panes.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineLayout.tsx:304-340` — `handleBodyRightScroll` ALSO writes `transform: translateX(-${scrollLeft}px)` on the header pane's inner content wrapper to track horizontal scroll without a scroll container of its own. `overflow: hidden + transform` produces zero scrollbar on the header band (parity-stable visual).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/ResourceTimelineLayout.tsx:127-138` — `gantt-timeline-divider` lives in column 2 of the 3-column grid, spans `1 / 3` row range. No sticky positioning needed under dual-scrollport (divider sits naturally between sidebar + chart grid tracks).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/internal-common/RegistryConfigImpl.ts:48-67` — `stickyHeader: true` default. The non-sticky branch collapses to single-scroll behavior chronix doesn't need to model.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 23)

- **`scrollingPaneRef` guard is load-bearing**: without it, every programmatic `scrollTop` write fires a scroll event on the target pane, which writes back to the source, ad infinitum. The "first-to-fire wins + rAF reset" pattern is robust across mouse wheel, scrollbar drag, AND programmatic `element.scrollTo()`. chronix's `useScrollSync` implements the same guard via a `ref<'a' | 'b' | null>` source flag; rAF reset clears it after each forwarded write.
- **`transform: translateX` not `scrollLeft` for header sync**: the chart-header pane uses `overflow: hidden` (no scrollbar visible) + the inner content wrapper gets a `translateX(-${pane.scrollLeft}px)` update on every body-pane scroll event. The reverse (`overflow: scroll + scrollLeft`) would either show a redundant header scrollbar (if visible) or fight with the body-pane's scrollbar layout. Visual parity demands the header has NO scrollbar — it's an axis display, not a scroll surface.
- **Vue 3 template-ref nullification bug** (mid-phase finding): the composables initially read `paneRef.value?.removeEventListener(...)` inside `onUnmounted`, but Vue 3 nullifies template refs BEFORE `onUnmounted` fires. The optional chain always bailed, leaving listeners attached on every mount/unmount cycle — a slow leak invisible to the green-test signal. Fix: capture the resolved element at `onMounted` time into a closure-scope variable; `onUnmounted` uses the captured reference. Applied to all three composables (`useScrollSync`, `useChartScrollState`, inline `useHeaderHorizontalSync`).
- **Pointer math unchanged**: chronix's existing `toContentXY(e)` reads `bodySvg.getBoundingClientRect()` which the browser auto-adjusts for the chart-pane's scroll. So `e.clientX - rect.left` still produces the correct content-x even when `chartPane.scrollLeft > 0` (the SVG's `rect.left` becomes negative, encoding the scroll-shift). Same model as Phase 4.5; no formula change.
- **`useChartScrollState` is the future-consumer hook** (chronix-additive): exposes `{ scrollLeft, clientWidth }` reactive refs derived from a `scroll` listener + ResizeObserver. Phase 23 itself doesn't consume the state visually — it just exposes the hook for Phase 27.1 (PlacedBar viewport-clipping flags) and Phase 28.2.1 (text-area-by-viewport-width truncation) to thread when those follow-ups land.
- **Sticky positioning becomes dead code** under dual-scrollport: the existing `position: sticky; top: 0` on chart-header (Phase 4.5), `position: sticky; left: 0` on sidebar-header / sidebar-body (Phase 5), and `position: sticky; left: ${sidebarWidth}px` on the divider (Phase 14) are all removed. Each pane sits in its own grid cell; sticky positioning was a workaround for the single-scrollport architecture and isn't needed when each pane owns its scroll.
- **Wrapper itself loses `overflow: auto`**: the wrapper becomes a pure CSS grid container. Both `hasSidebar=true` (3-column grid) and `hasSidebar=false` (1-column grid) cases use the same model — chart-header-pane sits above chart-pane in row 1/row 2 of the grid; sidebar-header-pane + sidebar-pane render only when sidebar columns are configured.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 23)

- `adapters/vue3/src/use-scroll-sync.ts` (new, ~75 LOC): `useScrollSync(paneA, paneB)` composable. Bidirectional `scrollTop` sync with `ref<'a' | 'b' | null>` source guard + rAF reset. Captures element refs on mount for cleanup-safe removeEventListener calls.
- `adapters/vue3/src/use-scroll-sync.test.ts` (new, ~120 LOC, +6 tests): mount/unmount cleanup, A→B + B→A sync, source-guard prevents writeback, rAF reset allows next scroll fresh from either side, null refs safe.
- `adapters/vue3/src/use-chart-scroll-state.ts` (new, ~70 LOC): `useChartScrollState(paneRef)` → `{ scrollLeft, clientWidth }` reactive refs. Scroll listener + ResizeObserver. Same captured-ref cleanup pattern.
- `adapters/vue3/src/use-chart-scroll-state.test.ts` (new, ~135 LOC, +5 tests): initial state, scrollLeft updates on scroll event, clientWidth updates on ResizeObserver fire (MockResizeObserver), reactive ref consumer pattern, cleanup on unmount.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (~210 LOC modified): new `maxBodyHeight?: string` prop (defaults `undefined`); 4 new refs (chartPaneRef / chartHeaderInnerRef / sidebarPaneRef / sidebarHeaderInnerRef); inline `useHeaderHorizontalSync` helper + invocations for both panes; `useScrollSync(sidebarPaneRef, chartPaneRef)` + `useChartScrollState(chartPaneRef)` wired in setup; `scrollToDateImpl` updated to write `chartPaneRef.value.scrollLeft`; structural wrapper restructure (5-flat-children → 6 panes: sidebar-header-pane + chart-header-pane + sidebar-pane + chart-pane + divider, each with grid placement + own overflow); 3 sticky-position style blobs removed (sidebar-header / sidebar-body / chart-header) + 1 partial removal (divider sticky-left).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-dual-scrollport.test.ts` (new, ~160 LOC, +10 tests): sidebar + chart pane presence (with/without `:columns`); chart-pane vs chart-header-pane overflow; sidebar-pane vs sidebar-header-pane overflow; grid template rows includes maxBodyHeight; chart-header-inner `willChange: transform`; chart-pane scrollLeft → chart-header-inner translateX; sidebar-pane scrollLeft → sidebar-header-inner translateX; chart-pane vertical scroll mirrors to sidebar-pane via useScrollSync.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.test.ts` (~10 LOC modified across 8 existing test updates): removed sticky-style assertions on chart-header / sidebar-header / sidebar-body / divider; replaced with new dual-scrollport DOM assertions (pane existence, overflow values, grid template).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-handle.test.ts` (~5 LOC modified): `scrollToDate` test now reads chart-pane's scrollLeft instead of wrapper's.
- `adapters/vue3/src/index.ts` (+4 exports): `useScrollSync`, `useChartScrollState`, `ChartScrollState`, `HeaderCellArg`/`HeaderCellClassNamesFunc` (Phase 29 re-exports that should have shipped then; added in Phase 23 cleanup pass).
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/App.vue` (+1 line): `max-body-height="70vh"` on `<ChronixGantt>` to engage dual-scrollport vertical scroll in the demo.
- `examples/gantt-vue3/src/styles.css` (~5 LOC modified): removed dead `.cx-gantt-wrapper { max-height: 70vh }` CSS override (wrapper no longer owns scroll); replaced with comment explaining the new architecture.
- `tooling/golden-runner/src/reference-dom-map.ts` (+11 LOC): new `TIMELINE_BODY_LEFT = '.gantt-timeline-body-left'` selector export with JSDoc explaining the dual-scrollport mapping.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+~135 LOC, +2 parity assertions): `phase23-dual-scrollport DOM presence parity` (both sides emit 2 overflow: auto scroll containers per `getComputedStyle`) + `phase23-vertical-scroll-sync lockstep parity` (programmatic scrollTo on chart-pane mirrors to sidebar-pane within rAF + 1px on both sides). Also updates `phase24-handle.scrollToDate` to read chart-pane scrollLeft instead of wrapper.
- **VRT impact**: 20 PNG re-baseline (vs design's 32-PNG estimate). 5 chronix-visual + 15 vrt-_ chronix-side cross-demo. 12 cross-_ k-ui-side baselines unchanged (k-ui rendering didn't change). First non-zero-VRT phase since Phase 26 (Phase 27 / 28.1 / 28.3 / 29 were all 0-VRT); justified by the genuine structural change.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 23)

- **Vue 3 template-ref nullification before onUnmounted** (CRITICAL load-bearing finding): initially wrote composables with `paneRef.value?.removeEventListener(...)` inside `onUnmounted`. Test surfaced via `expect(removeSpy).toHaveBeenCalled() — Number of calls: 0`. Investigation: Vue 3 lifecycle is `onBeforeUnmount → DOM removal → ref nullification → onUnmounted`. By the time onUnmounted fires, `paneRef.value === null` and the optional chain bails. The listener was never removed; the addEventListener call from `onMounted` leaked once per mount. Fix: capture the resolved element at mount time into a closure-scope variable; cleanup uses the captured reference. Applied to all 3 composables (`useScrollSync`, `useChartScrollState`, inline `useHeaderHorizontalSync`). **This bug would have been invisible without the explicit cleanup-spy test** — the leak is silent, only surfacing as growing memory in long-running apps.
- **String-ref auto-binding doesn't work with setup-returned refs** (composable test churn): initial test scaffold used `<div ref="paneA">` in `render()` to bind into a setup-returned `paneA` Ref. String-refs populate `this.$refs.paneA` (Options API instance scope), NOT the setup-scope ref object the composable closes over. Fix: switch to function-style render (return a render closure from setup; pass the Ref object directly into the `ref:` prop), which Vue auto-binds via the composition-API contract.
- **Existing test churn from sticky removal** (8 tests in chronix-gantt.test.ts): pre-Phase-23 tests asserted on `style.position === 'sticky'`, `style.top === '0px'`, `style.left === '0px'`, `style.zIndex` ladders. All became invalid under dual-scrollport. Bulk-replaced each with the new dual-scrollport assertion (pane existence + overflow value + grid placement). Pattern: sticky-style assertions on layout helpers tend to be the most fragile category; consider asserting on the DOM-structural invariant (which pane wraps which content) rather than the positioning model that delivers it.
- **MockResizeObserver lint cleanup** (3-iteration fix): vitest doesn't ship a ResizeObserver mock; tests stubbed `globalThis.ResizeObserver`. Initial TS-narrowed `let observerCallback: ResizeObserverCallback | null = null` failed because TS flow analysis didn't see the constructor assignment. Switched to a holder object `{ cb: ResizeObserverCallback | undefined }`. ESLint then flagged empty `observe()` / `unobserve()` / `disconnect()` mock methods — added `// mock-only; no-op` comments to suppress. Final iteration: dropped the unnecessary `as unknown as typeof ResizeObserver` cast (single `as typeof ResizeObserver` suffices in jsdom-friendly contexts).
- **Phase 24 handle.scrollToDate assertion + adapter unit test stale**: both asserted on `wrapper.scrollLeft` (pre-Phase-23 contract). Updated to read chart-pane's scrollLeft. Pattern: phase-introduced contract changes that move state ownership require sweep of all assertion sites that READ that state — the impl change + the test update must land in the same commit OR the test fails as a regression on the next ci-check.
- **Port 8702 lingering vite dev server**: Phase 23 needed a fresh restart of the chronix demo dev server to pick up the new `@chronixjs/gantt-vue3` dist (vite caches the resolved module across HMR). Discovered when first capture attempt produced no diffs vs old baselines — the stale-dist symptom. Fix: explicit `netstat -ano | grep :8702` + `Stop-Process` before relaunch.

### Naming justifications (Phase 23)

- **`cx-gantt-sidebar-pane` / `cx-gantt-chart-pane`** (vs k-ui's geometric `body-left` / `body-right`): chronix uses feature-name prefixes for pane identification (`sidebar` for the resource panel, `chart` for the timeline body). The k-ui geometric names assume LTR + the resource panel sits left; chronix's naming is RTL-neutral. Symmetric with `cx-gantt-sidebar-header` (Phase 5) + `cx-gantt-chart-header` (implicit Phase 4.5) — no new mental model.
- **`cx-gantt-sidebar-header-pane` / `cx-gantt-chart-header-pane`** (wrapper with `overflow: hidden`): `-pane` suffix marks the OUTER scroll-container shell; the inner content sits in `*-inner` wrappers. Distinction matters because the `translateX` listener targets the inner element, not the pane itself.
- **`cx-gantt-sidebar-header-inner` / `cx-gantt-chart-header-inner`** (inner translateX target): `-inner` suffix matches the parity reference's `gantt-timeline-header-wrapper` naming (k-ui calls it `-wrapper`; chronix uses `-inner` to avoid collision with `cx-gantt-wrapper` which is the top-level grid container).
- **`useScrollSync`** (composable, vs `useBidirectionalScrollSync` / `useDualPaneSync`): the simpler name describes WHAT (sync) without implementation details (bidirectional vs one-way; pane count). The single-purpose composable accepts two refs — caller-side ergonomic without verbose name.
- **`useChartScrollState`** (composable, vs `useChartPaneScroll` / `useScrollLeftAndWidth`): `State` (singular) instead of method-name-style. Returns a struct of refs (`{ scrollLeft, clientWidth }`) so the future-additive case of more derived state (e.g. `isScrolledToStart`, `viewportTimeRange`) doesn't require breaking the API.
- **`ChartScrollState`** (interface, vs `ScrollState` / `ChartScroll`): `Chart` prefix because the composable is chart-pane-specific (it doesn't sync; it observes). Distinguishes from `useScrollSync`'s bidirectional model conceptually.
- **`maxBodyHeight`** (prop, vs `bodyHeight` / `chartHeight` / `paneHeight`): "body" matches the existing `bodyHeight` derivation in setup (post-strip-layout content height); "max" signals it's a cap, not an exact height (panes can be shorter if content fits). Accepts CSS length string — no type narrowing on `auto` / `1fr` / `%` / `vh`.
- **`scrollSyncSource`** (was the design's name for the guard ref; renamed `source` in implementation): the design proposed `scrollSyncSource: Ref<'sidebar' | 'chart' | null>`. Implementation uses `source: Ref<'a' | 'b' | null>` because the composable is generic (any 2 panes, not specifically sidebar/chart). The lift to a generic shape lets external consumers reuse `useScrollSync` for non-sidebar/chart pairs (e.g. two scrollable lists).
- **`TIMELINE_BODY_LEFT`** (selector constant in reference-dom-map.ts): kept the k-ui geometric name (`body-left`) because it's the LITERAL CSS class on the parity reference's DOM. The chronix-side mapping (`cx-gantt-sidebar-pane`) is documented in the JSDoc.

### Open / parked (Phase 23)

- **`setAutoScrollEnabled(false)` while divider drags** (parity reference's autoScroll-suppression during divider drag) — parked. chronix has no auto-scroll feature (K.7 RENDER_LAYER_GAP_SWEEP item: ⏸️ defer-indefinite). Re-prioritize when auto-scroll lands.
- **Phase 27.1 viewport clipping** (PlacedBar `isClippedStart` / `isClippedEnd` flags via chart-pane scrollLeft + clientWidth) — UNBLOCKED by Phase 23's `useChartScrollState` exposure; not consumed yet. Re-prioritize once the user requests viewport-aware continuation triangles or text truncation.
- **Phase 28.2.1 text-area-by-viewport-width truncation** — same. The composable hook is in place; downstream consumption is a separate phase.
- **Horizontal sidebar scroll** (when columns sum > sidebar pane width) — works automatically under dual-scrollport (sidebar-pane has `overflow: auto`). Not test-covered in cross-demo because chronix's parity-mode demo doesn't have wide sidebars; consumer-facing pattern is in the design doc.
- **`dualScrollport?: boolean` opt-out flag** — REJECTED per design decision #3. chronix pre-1.0 + clean-replacement + no flag-gating + 20-PNG VRT re-baseline accepted.
- **Cross-demo horizontal scroll-sync test** (drive `chartPane.scrollLeft = 100`, assert chart-header-inner's `transform` matches and the sidebar-pane's scrollLeft stays at 0) — parked. Pinned by adapter unit tests; cross-demo parity for horizontal sync is structurally equivalent to vertical (both use the same `useScrollSync` mechanism), so adding a second parity assertion mostly duplicates the first.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 23)

Design-doc estimate: 7.5h, ~1530 LOC + 32 PNGs. Actual:

- Commit 1 (`25b065a`) design: 661 LOC (close to ~700 estimate; prettier reformatted wide tables).
- Commit 2 (`8402366`) adapter: 859 LOC across 8 files (3 new src files + 3 new test files + 2 modified). On budget (~710 LOC estimated; over by ~150 due to the structural test churn + the captured-ref bug fix expansion).
- Commit 3 (`f17688b`) demo + VRT: 22 files changed (~7 LOC + 20 PNGs). 20-PNG re-baseline vs design's 32-PNG prediction (12 cross-\* baselines stayed valid because k-ui rendering didn't change).
- Commit 4 (`3ffa838`) parity assertions + Phase 24 handle test fix: 170 LOC across 3 files. Slightly over the ~90 estimate due to the Phase 24 follow-on fix (wasn't in the original Commit 4 scope but surfaced from the full-verify run and was bundled in to avoid splitting the commit).
- Commit 5 (wrap-up): this commit.
- **Total**: ~1730 LOC across 4 commits in ~6 hours (under 7.5h estimate). VRT re-baseline 20 PNGs (vs 32 predicted) because k-ui side stayed pixel-identical.

**Verdict**: single-session discipline held. The Vue-template-ref nullification bug was the load-bearing discovery — would have been a silent memory leak in long-running apps without the explicit cleanup-spy test in Commit 2's `use-scroll-sync.test.ts`. The "captured ref at mount time" pattern is now precedent for all chronix composables that attach event listeners. **Dual-scrollport architecture unblocks Phase 27.1 + 28.2.1 viewport-aware features as designed**; their wiring is now a small follow-up, not a structural re-engineering.

## Phase 25 — drag-distance gate (5px Pythagorean) (DONE, 2026-05-18)

Closes chronix's pre-Phase-25 strict-zero-delta divergence from the parity reference (tracked at `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md:135` as 🟡): a 1-4 px pointer "wiggle" between pointerdown + pointerup used to commit a sub-threshold drag / resize / select on chronix but is suppressed as a click on the reference. Phase 25 adds the Pythagorean distance threshold gate the reference's `FeaturefulElementDragging.ts` has had since forever, restoring parity for sub-threshold gestures. User-approved scope **A** (single shared `pointerMinDistance`, default 5 px) / **A** (composable-level gate with sticky `dragDistanceSurpassedFlag`) / **A** (uniform 5 px for all pointer types).

### Reference reading (Phase 25)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/interaction/dnd/FeaturefulElementDragging.ts:101-125` — `onPointerMove` computes `distanceSq = deltaX*deltaX + deltaY*deltaY` and calls `handleDistanceSurpassed(ev)` once `distanceSq >= minDistance * minDistance`. Squared comparison avoids `Math.sqrt`.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/interaction/dnd/FeaturefulElementDragging.ts:127-146` — `onPointerUp` short-circuits when `isDragging === false`. No dragend / drop fires; the release is treated as a click.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/interaction/dnd/FeaturefulElementDragging.ts:158-167` — `handleDistanceSurpassed` is one of two conditions for `dragstart` (the other is delay-end; chronix has no delay concept). Default `delay=undefined` collapses to "distance only".
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/interaction/interactions/EventDragging.ts:687-693` — `eventDragMinDistance` defaults to 5.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/interaction/interactions/DateSelecting.ts` — `selectMinDistance` shares the same minDistance semantics; chronix v0 collapses both into a single shared `pointerMinDistance`.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 25)

- **Sticky "ever surpassed" semantics**: the threshold check fires per-pointermove, but the flag must be sticky. If the user moves to distance 6 (surpasses threshold → drag confirmed) then drifts back to distance 3, the transaction's CURRENT deltaX/deltaY reflect distance 3 (sub-threshold). The drag IS still confirmed because the threshold was surpassed at some point. K-ui's `isDistanceSurpassed: boolean` instance field captures this; chronix mirrors via `dragDistanceSurpassedFlag: Ref<boolean>` in composable scope.
- **Composable-scope `lastBeginPx` for all 4 kinds**: `CalendarRangeSelectTransaction` lacks `deltaX`/`deltaY` pixel fields (its shape is time-domain). So the distance check can't read from the transaction shape alone. Solution: capture the pointerdown content-x/y at `begin()` into a composable-scope `lastBeginPx: Ref<{ x, y } | null>`; `advance()` computes distance from there. Applies uniformly across all 4 transaction kinds.
- **Phase 16 lazy-fire gate becomes the threshold gate**: existing `dragStartFired` latch (Phase 16) was "first non-zero delta fires dragStart". Phase 25 adds a SECOND precondition: `dragStartFired.value === false && dragDistanceSurpassedFlag.value === true`. Sub-threshold gestures never flip the sticky flag → dragStart never fires → symmetric dragStop also never fires → reference protocol parity preserved (no orphan dragStart-without-dragStop emits).
- **Squared-distance comparison preserves the reference's exact idiom**: `dx*dx + dy*dy >= minDistance * minDistance` is verbatim from `FeaturefulElementDragging.ts:108`. Skips `Math.sqrt`.
- **Adapter's `onPointerup` migrates from `isNoOpDrag` to `isSubThresholdGesture`**: pre-Phase-25 the check was `(deltaX === 0 && deltaY === 0)` per kind. Phase 25 replaces with `!pointer.dragDistanceSurpassed.value && txn.kind !== 'progress-handle'`. Progress-handle stays exempted: reaching the handle hit zone IS the intent (matches reference + chronix pre-Phase-25 progress behavior).
- **Default 5 px matches reference**: k-ui's `minDistance` default is 5; chronix's `pointerMinDistance` prop defaults to 5. Setting to 0 restores the pre-Phase-25 strict-zero gate for consumers who relied on that behavior.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 25)

- `adapters/vue3/src/use-gantt-pointer.ts` (~50 LOC modified):
  - `UseGanttPointerInput`: new `pointerMinDistance?: MaybeRefOrGetter<number>` (default 5, applies to all 4 transaction kinds).
  - `UseGanttPointerOutput`: new `dragDistanceSurpassed: ComputedRef<boolean>` reactive ref.
  - Setup scope: new `dragDistanceSurpassedFlag: Ref<boolean>` sticky flag + `lastBeginPx: Ref<{ x, y } | null>` pointerdown-origin capture.
  - `begin(contentX, contentY)`: resets `dragDistanceSurpassedFlag = false` + captures `lastBeginPx = { x: contentX, y: contentY }`.
  - `advance(contentX, contentY)`: end-of-block computes `dx*dx + dy*dy` against `lastBeginPx`; flips flag when `>= minDistance * minDistance`.
  - Phase 16 lazy-fire `dragStartFired` gate gains `&& dragDistanceSurpassedFlag.value` precondition; inner non-zero-delta check dropped (subsumed by distance check).
- `adapters/vue3/src/use-gantt-pointer.test.ts` (+~155 LOC, +6 tests in new `describe('useGanttPointer — Phase 25 drag-distance gate')`).
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (~20 LOC modified): new `pointerMinDistance: { type: Number, default: 5 }` prop; threaded into composable; `onPointerup`'s `isNoOpDrag` check replaced with `isSubThresholdGesture`.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-drag-distance.test.ts` (new, ~165 LOC, +6 tests): sub-threshold bar-body wiggle fires `bar-click` not `bar-drop`, above-threshold fires `bar-drop` not `bar-click`, `pointerMinDistance=0` restores pre-Phase-25 behavior, sub-threshold resize gesture doesn't commit a resize, sub-threshold select gesture doesn't commit + fires `empty-area-click`, progress-handle commits regardless of distance.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (+~85 LOC, +1 parity assertion): `phase25-sub-threshold pointer wiggle does NOT commit a drag on either side (3 px wiggle, week view)` — locates `event-1` on both sides, captures bbox.left, drives a 3-px mouse wiggle via `page.mouse`, re-reads bbox.left, asserts delta ≤ 1 px. Result: kui Δ=0.00px chronix Δ=0.00px (both gates fired correctly).
- `tooling/golden-runner/src/reference-dom-map.ts`: `EVENT_BAR` already existed (line 71); no new selectors needed.
- **VRT impact**: zero re-baseline. 27/27 cross-demo verify green; 5/5 chronix-visual baselines unchanged. Phase 25 is purely a runtime gesture-handling adjustment — no DOM emission changes.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 25)

- **Adapter click-path only fires bar-click for `bar-body` hits, not `bar-edge` hits** (test design correction): initial draft of the sub-threshold-edge-gesture test asserted that a sub-threshold gesture on the bar's edge would fire `bar-click`. False: the adapter's click-emit branch in `onPointerup` reads `lastHit.kind` and only fires `bar-click` for `bar-body` (and `empty-area-click` for `empty-row`). Edge hits are silently dropped on sub-threshold. Adjusted test to assert only the load-bearing invariant (no bar-resize commit); edge-click follow-up is a separate parity concern, not in Phase 25 scope.
- **No existing test asserted sub-threshold commits** (relief): grep across all 3 adapter test files returned no matches. The 0-VRT-impact / 0-existing-test-update outcome was the design's optimistic prediction; reality matched.
- **Background dev-server lifecycle**: parity-spec needs both demos up; killed dangling chronix demo via `netstat -ano | Stop-Process` precondition before each run. Same pattern as Phase 23.

### Naming justifications (Phase 25)

- **`pointerMinDistance`** (vs `dragMinDistance` / `eventDragMinDistance` / `minDistance`): "pointer" prefix because the threshold applies to ALL pointer gestures (drag + resize + select + progress), not just "drag". chronix's existing `useGanttPointer` composable name uses "pointer" as the umbrella term; the prop name follows. "min distance" matches reference's `minDistance` field for instant recognizability.
- **`dragDistanceSurpassed`** (output ref name, vs `isDistanceSurpassed` / `pointerDistanceSurpassed`): "drag" prefix for output ref because the consumer-side semantic is "this gesture has crossed the threshold to become a drag". Public-API readers see `pointer.dragDistanceSurpassed.value` and immediately understand its role.
- **`dragDistanceSurpassedFlag`** (private scope variable name, suffix `Flag`): the `Flag` suffix mirrors existing `dragCommittedFlag` and `dragStartFired` siblings in the composable scope — consistent local naming convention for booleans that track gesture lifecycle state.
- **`lastBeginPx`** (origin tracker name, vs `pointerDownPx` / `beginOrigin` / `originPx`): "last" because it's the latest pointerdown's origin (one per gesture lifetime); "begin" matches the composable's `begin()` method name; "Px" suffix marks pixel-space. Disambiguates from each transaction shape's own `originPx` field (which is per-transaction, not per-composable-instance).
- **`isSubThresholdGesture`** (adapter local var name, vs `isNoOpDrag` / `isSubThresholdDrag` / `belowThreshold`): renamed from pre-Phase-25 `isNoOpDrag` because the semantic is broader now ("below threshold" includes the strict-zero case but also 1-4 px wiggles). "Gesture" instead of "Drag" because the check applies to all 4 transaction kinds.

### Open / parked (Phase 25)

- **Per-transaction-kind thresholds** (reference's `eventDragMinDistance` vs `selectMinDistance` separation) — parked. Single shared `pointerMinDistance` covers the parity-restoration goal. Re-prioritize on consumer demand for kind-specific thresholds.
- **Per-pointer-type thresholds** (touch=0 vs mouse=5 mirroring reference's per-type defaults) — parked. chronix v0 has no `PointerEvent.pointerType` plumbing anywhere. Bundle with `eventLongPressDelay` defer-indefinite cluster when long-press support lands.
- **Time-based delay gate** (reference's `delay` setTimeout-driven gate before dragstart) — REJECTED. chronix has no delay / lifecycle-hook concept anywhere. Architectural drift to add one composable's setTimeout. Re-prioritize when long-press + chronix lifecycle-hook stories converge.
- **Axis-locked drags** (reference's `applyOnTrack` / `track` enum for X-only or Y-only drag mode) — parked. No chronix axis-lock surface; defer-indefinite.
- **Edge-hit click-emit** (when a sub-threshold gesture on a bar's edge resolves, should `bar-click` fire for the underlying bar?) — parked. Separate parity concern; not in Phase 25 scope. Re-prioritize on consumer report.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 25)

- Commit 1 (`97ab13b`) design: 522 LOC (over ~450 estimate; prettier reformatted wide tables + a `>=` paragraph that got mis-parsed as a blockquote, harmless).
- Commit 2 (`412ff47`) composable + adapter + 12 tests: 428 LOC across 4 files (~70 LOC src + ~360 LOC tests + comments). On budget.
- Commit 3 (`cae10c6`) parity assertion: 84 LOC. On budget.
- Commit 4 (wrap-up): this commit.
- **Total**: ~1100 LOC across 3 commits in ~2.5 hours (under 3.5h estimate). Zero VRT churn — first 0-VRT phase since Phase 23 broke the streak; pattern restored.

**Verdict**: single-session discipline held. The sticky-flag design choice was the load-bearing decision — without it, a hysteresis case (surpass then drift back) would have failed the threshold-protocol invariant. The Phase 16 lazy-fire gate integration was clean: just add a second precondition to an existing latch, no protocol-violation paths possible. **Pre-Phase-25 strict-zero-delta divergence CLOSED**.

## Phase 27.1 — viewport-clipping flags + viewport-edge continuation triangles (DONE, 2026-05-18)

First consumer of Phase 23's `useChartScrollState` composable; extends Phase 27 (DONE 2026-05-16, axis-clipped continuation triangles) with chronix-additive viewport-clipped triangles that fire dynamically on user scroll. Apex locks to the visible viewport edge in content-coords so the indicator stays at the viewport edge regardless of how far the bar has scrolled offscreen. User-approved scope **B** (render-time derivation via pure helper, no PlacedBar shape change) / **A** (test surface: 8 pure-helper unit tests + 5 SFC reactivity tests via jsdom programmatic scroll) / **A** (title + progress-dot adapter deferred to planned Phase 28.2.1). Mid-implementation correction: prop-plumbing trace revealed k-ui's `<TimelineEvent containerWidth>` carries axis content width (not viewport width), so Phase 27.1 is **chronix-additive**, not a port — flipped from cross-demo parity to chronix-new declaration.

### Reference reading (Phase 27.1)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:24` — `containerWidth?: number` declared on TimelineEvent prop interface.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:286-298` — the `containerWidth`-driven check: `isClippedStart = x < 0 || !isEventStart; isClippedEnd = x + finalWidth > containerWidth || !isEventEnd;`. Surface-level reads as "viewport-clipping check" but the value of `containerWidth` makes it redundant with axis-clipping (see Mechanisms).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:313-348` — triangle position branch: viewport-locked apex when `isClipped*` fires (`(triangleMargin, centerY)` / `(containerWidth - triangleMargin, centerY)`), bar-edge anchored apex otherwise.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:1542` — **load-bearing finding**: `containerWidth={timelineWidth}` where `timelineWidth = calculateTimelineWidth(tDateProfile) = slotCount × slotMinWidth`. **k-ui's `containerWidth` is axis content width, NOT visible viewport width.**
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/resource-timeline/GanttView.tsx:1471-1472` — independent corroboration: `isClippedStart = hcoords.start < 0; isClippedEnd = hcoords.end > timelineWidth;` then maps onto `modifiedSeg.isStart`/`isEnd`. The viewport-clipped check at TimelineEvent.tsx:286-298 is algebraically equivalent to `!isEventStart` / `!isEventEnd` when `containerWidth = timelineWidth`.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineLane.tsx:246` — alternate plumbing path: `containerWidth = props.timelineCoords?.outerCoordCache?.originClientRect?.width`. `getBoundingClientRect().width` of the timeline-content element (full-stretched at content width), not the visible viewport portion. Also content width.
- `d:/work/chronix/audit/PHASE_27_CONTINUATION_INDICATORS_DESIGN.md:73, 237-238, 480-483` — Phase 27 explicitly deferred viewport-clipping work pointing to "Phase 23 + 23.1 follow-up". This phase realizes that deferred work, retroactively reclassified as chronix-additive after the prop-plumbing trace.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 27.1)

- **k-ui's `containerWidth` is content width, not viewport width**: k-ui does NOT emit additional triangles when the user scrolls horizontally. Its triangle count is invariant under chart-pane scroll. The `x < 0 || x + finalWidth > containerWidth` check at TimelineEvent.tsx:286-298 is algebraically redundant with the `!isEventStart`/`!isEventEnd` check it OR's against (when `containerWidth = timelineWidth`, the OR's right operand is implied by the left). chronix's Phase 27.1 viewport-clipped triangles therefore have **no k-ui counterpart**; they are a UX enhancement, not a port.
- **Render-time derivation pattern** (Decision B, recommended): viewport-clipping is render-state, not layout-pipeline state. Pushing `scrollLeft` + `clientWidth` into `BarPlacementPass` (Decision A, rejected) would force layout re-runs on every scroll tick (O(n_bars) per frame) AND break the established "layout consumes layout-only inputs" boundary (Phase 2 architectural decision, never violated). The pure helper `deriveViewportClipping(renderX, renderWidth, scrollLeft, clientWidth, triangleMargin) → ViewportClippingResult` co-locates with the per-bar render closure that already consumes drag-aware geometry. Reactive via Vue's natural ref-dependency tracking on `chartScroll.scrollLeft.value` + `chartScroll.clientWidth.value`. Zero PlacedBar shape change → zero fixture churn → zero core test impact. Same simplification pattern as Phase 29's render-time-from-`tick.time` derivation (also zero PlannedAxis change).
- **`clientWidth === 0` pre-mount short-circuit is load-bearing**: before the chart-pane's `ResizeObserver` fires its first measurement, `clientWidth = 0`. Without the guard, `viewportRight = scrollLeft + 0 = scrollLeft` would erroneously flag every bar whose right edge exceeds `scrollLeft` as viewport-clipped-right → phantom triangles on initial render. The helper's `if (clientWidth === 0) return both-false` branch matches the parity reference's `containerWidth === undefined` short-circuit semantically (same "no viewport info → skip viewport check" pattern, different shape).
- **Strict `<` / `>` boundary semantics**: a bar whose left edge sits EXACTLY at `scrollLeft` is NOT viewport-clipped (the edge sits on the first visible pixel). Symmetric on the right. Established via the strict-boundary unit test.
- **Precedence (viewport-locked apex wins when both sub-cases fire on same side)**: when a bar is BOTH axis-clipped AND viewport-clipped on the same side (common in narrow viewports — e.g. chronix day-view at 800-px pane vs 1440-px axis), the apex locks to the viewport edge (Phase 27.1 wins). Matches the parity reference's first-branch-wins logic at TimelineEvent.tsx:314-320. To preserve Phase 27 axis-clipped parity assertions under this precedence, both sub-cases tag the polygon with INDEPENDENT data attributes (see Bugs / gotchas below).
- **Dual data-attribute model for cross-demo parity**: every triangle carries TWO independent booleans on the same polygon — `data-axis-clipped` (Phase 27 sub-case, `!bar.isStart` / `!bar.isEnd`) and `data-viewport-clipped` (Phase 27.1 sub-case). Apex precedence determines which sub-case visually wins, but BOTH attributes remain visible to consumer CSS / cross-demo parity tests. Phase 27 parity assertions filter chronix's selector to `[data-axis-clipped="true"]` so the chronix-additive sub-case doesn't inflate the k-ui-equivalent count.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 27.1)

- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-viewport-clipping.ts` (new, 69 LOC): pure helper `deriveViewportClipping(renderX, renderWidth, scrollLeft, clientWidth, triangleMargin) → ViewportClippingResult`. No Vue reactivity, no DOM dependency. `clientWidth=0` short-circuit. Strict `<` / `>` boundaries. Apex positions in content-coords.
- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-viewport-clipping.test.ts` (new, ~70 LOC, +8 tests): no-clip baseline, left-only, right-only, both flags fire, `clientWidth=0` short-circuit, viewport-locked left apex formula, viewport-locked right apex formula, strict-`<` boundary.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (~85 LOC modified):
  - Import `deriveViewportClipping`. Remove `eslint-disable-next-line @typescript-eslint/no-unused-vars` on `chartScroll` (Phase 23 wired it pre-emptively; Phase 27.1 is its first consumer).
  - Inside the per-bar `placedBars.value.flatMap` closure, after drag-aware `renderX` / `renderY` / `renderWidth`, compute `viewportClip = deriveViewportClipping(renderX, renderWidth, chartScroll.scrollLeft.value, chartScroll.clientWidth.value, TRIANGLE_MARGIN)`.
  - Rewrite Phase 27 triangle emit blocks. Fire condition becomes `!bar.isStart || viewportClip.isViewportClippedStart` (left) / `!bar.isEnd || viewportClip.isViewportClippedEnd` (right). Apex precedence: viewport-locked when `isViewportClipped*` fires (`scrollLeft + TRIANGLE_MARGIN` / `scrollLeft + clientWidth - TRIANGLE_MARGIN`), otherwise bar-edge anchored (`renderX + TRIANGLE_MARGIN` / `renderX + renderWidth - TRIANGLE_MARGIN`).
  - Each polygon emit gains TWO data attributes: `data-axis-clipped` (mirrors `!bar.isStart` / `!bar.isEnd` independently) and `data-viewport-clipped` (mirrors `isViewportClipped*` independently). Both are visible to consumer CSS + cross-demo parity probes regardless of which sub-case wins apex precedence.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-viewport-clipping.test.ts` (new, ~200 LOC, +5 tests): mounts ChronixGantt with stubbed `ResizeObserver` so SFC tests can deterministically fire viewport-state updates. Tests cover axis-only-clipped + `data-viewport-clipped="false"` at bar edge; viewport-only-clipped + `data-viewport-clipped="true"` at viewport edge; both-clipped same-side precedence (viewport-locked wins, apex at scrollLeft+1); scroll event re-derives count reactively; pre-mount `clientWidth=0` does not emit phantom triangles.
- `tooling/golden-runner/tests/parity.spec.ts` (~30 LOC modified): 4 Phase 27 axis-clipped parity assertions updated to filter chronix's selector to `[data-axis-clipped="true"]`. Comment block at the first assertion documents the dual-attribute pattern + the Phase 27.1 chronix-new rationale. All 4 assertions back to green: kui=10 chronix=10 (day-left), kui=13 chronix=13 (day-right), kui=6 chronix=6 (week-left), kui=5 chronix=5 (month-total).
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md`: P3 section gains a row for Phase 27.1 viewport-clipped triangles (chronix-additive, by-design rejection, pinning via 8 helper + 5 SFC tests). "Reject (by-design)" tally updated 8 → 9.
- `audit/PHASE_27_1_VIEWPORT_CLIPPING_DESIGN.md`: "Parity assertion plan" section rewritten to declare chronix-new. Original cross-demo assertion plan preserved verbatim under a STALE/superseded header for post-mortem audit traceability.
- **VRT re-baseline**: 15/27 cross-demo scenarios (all chronix-side `vrt-*.png`). 12 k-ui-side scenarios (`cross-*.png`) unchanged binary-identical (k-ui's triangle count is scroll-invariant). 5/5 chronix-visual baselines unchanged (Playwright captures SVG element directly + ResizeObserver hasn't fired by capture time → `clientWidth=0` → viewport-clip short-circuits → only axis-clipped triangles emit, identical pre-Phase-27.1 baselines).

**Test count after Phase 27.1**:

- vitest: 684 → **697** (+13). Core: 329 unchanged. Adapter: 344 → 357 (+13: 8 pure-helper + 5 SFC viewport-clipping). Demo: 11 unchanged.
- ChronixTheme tokens: 50 unchanged.
