### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 27.1)

- **Initial SFC test geometry errors** (Commit 2): drafted "axis-clipped bar" test with a bar at hours -4..6 + scrollLeft=0 — but renderX=-240 < scrollLeft=0 → viewport-clipped left ALSO fires → `data-viewport-clipped` came back "true" not "false". Fixed by using a bar at hours 10..30 (axis-clipped RIGHT, renderX=600) in a generous viewport (clientWidth=2000); viewport-clipping doesn't fire on either side. Also fixed "viewport-spanning bar" test: bar at hours 1..3 (axis-inside) was too short to span a 600-px viewport — fixed by using hours 1..16 so renderX=60, renderWidth=900 → spans viewport [300, 900) on both sides.
- **k-ui's `containerWidth` is content width, not viewport width** (Commit 3, mid-implementation): prop-plumbing trace via `GanttView.tsx:1542 containerWidth={timelineWidth}` showed k-ui's `containerWidth` carries axis content width. This contradicted the design doc's "parity port" framing. Flipped to chronix-new declaration; 2 originally-planned cross-demo parity assertions REPLACED by chronix-additive declaration in `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` P3. Design doc's "Parity assertion plan" section rewritten with full correction rationale; original plan preserved under a STALE/superseded header for audit traceability.
- **Phase 27 parity assertions broke** (Commit 3): after the chronix-additive viewport-clipped triangles started emitting in real-browser day/week views (chart pane narrower than axis content), the 4 Phase 27 assertions failed. Initial fix attempt with `[data-viewport-clipped="false"]` filter matched ZERO triangles in chronix (precedence-rule means axis-clipped bars near edges ALSO get `data-viewport-clipped="true"`). Correct fix: add SEPARATE `data-axis-clipped` attribute on every triangle (independent of viewport-clipping precedence) and filter on that. Both attributes stay visible on the polygon; cross-demo parity uses axis flag.
- **Chronix dev server lifecycle**: parity-spec / cross-demo verify require chronix demo running on port 8702. Phase 23's `Stop-Process -Force` + restart pattern reused. On one re-run mid-Commit-3, the chronix dev server died (likely due to vite HMR caching stale dist files during the restart window); cross-demo verify ran 1.3min instead of 27s, 15 scenarios failed before chronix was confirmed dead. Resolution: kill + restart cleanly + wait on port-binding via `until netstat -ano | grep ':8702.*LISTENING'` before re-running tests.
- **Chronix-visual baselines unchanged**: predicted 4-5 of 5 re-captures; reality was 0. Theory: Playwright captures the SVG element directly + the ResizeObserver hasn't fired by capture time → `chartScroll.clientWidth.value = 0` → the helper's `clientWidth === 0` short-circuit returns both flags false → only axis-clipped triangles emit, matching the pre-Phase-27.1 baseline pixel-identically. Cross-demo VRT captures use a different code path that gives the chart-pane enough time to bind its ResizeObserver, hence the 15-PNG re-baseline there.

### Naming justifications (Phase 27.1)

- **`deriveViewportClipping`** (helper function name, vs `computeViewportClip` / `getViewportClipState`): "derive" matches the helper's role as a pure data transform; "Viewport" prefix scopes the concern; "Clipping" matches the established Phase 27 terminology (`continuation` / `clipped` interchangeable in this domain).
- **`ViewportClippingResult`** (return type name): captures the 4-field record. Singular "Result" matches existing chronix patterns like `BarPlacementOutput` / `AxisRangePlanResult`.
- **`isViewportClippedStart` / `isViewportClippedEnd`** (sub-flag names): "is" prefix for booleans; "ViewportClipped" disambiguates from Phase 27's `isStart` / `isEnd` axis-clipped semantics on `PlacedBar`. Pattern parallels k-ui's `isClippedStart` / `isClippedEnd` naming for ease of cross-reference.
- **`viewportLockedLeftApexX` / `viewportLockedRightApexX`** (apex coord output names): "viewport-locked" makes the precedence rule explicit in the API surface; "Apex" matches the geometric vocabulary established in Phase 27 (apex / base / centerY); "X" suffix marks content-coord pixel-space (consistent with `lastBeginPx`-style suffixes in Phase 25).
- **`data-axis-clipped` / `data-viewport-clipped`** (HTML data attributes): kebab-case per HTML convention; "axis" + "viewport" terms match the design doc's mental model + the helper's API; "clipped" reuses the established Phase 27 vocabulary. Independent booleans on the same polygon — both visible to cross-demo parity tests + consumer CSS.
- **`fireLeftTriangle` / `fireRightTriangle`** (local emit-gate var names): "fire" verb matches the boolean-condition pattern (`if (fire*) { ... emit ... }`); "Triangle" reads naturally in the context of polygon emit blocks. Disambiguates from the `isViewportClipped*` data flag (which describes a sub-case state, not an emit gate).

### Open / parked (Phase 27.1)

- **Title + progress-dot adapter for viewport-clipped triangles** — deferred to planned Phase 28.2.1. Phase 28.2's title-positioning logic (chronix-gantt.ts:2254-2270) currently shifts the title past `!bar.isStart` axis-clipped triangles only. Title may visually overlap the viewport-locked triangle on bars whose title is wider than the visible portion. Interim visual issue is small + reversible; Phase 28.2.1 will consume the same `deriveViewportClipping` helper to fix.
- **Touch-scroll-driven viewport-clipping parity** — parked. chronix v0 uniform pointer model uses native `overflow:auto`'s default touch handling; mouse + touch scroll exercise the same scroll-event path so the chronix-side behavior is structurally identical. No per-pointer-type composable surface to extend.
- **Per-bar viewport-locked apex-x snapshot in cross-demo parity** — parked. The chronix-new declaration removed the originally-planned cross-demo parity assertion entirely; internal SFC tests pin the apex formula directly (`expect(leftApex).toBe(301)` etc.). Re-prioritize if a consumer reports visual divergence under heavy horizontal scroll.

- ci-check fully green: format / lint / typecheck / test / build / audit:names (171 files) / audit:catalog (361 k-ui items × 49 audit files scanned).
- **Phase 27 viewport-clipping deferred-row CLOSED** (axis-clipped sub-case ported in Phase 27; viewport-clipped sub-case landed Phase 27.1 as chronix-additive). chronix now ships scroll-aware viewport-clipped triangles that fire dynamically on user scroll + chart-pane resize; apex locks to the visible viewport edge in content-coords. Triangle stays at viewport edge regardless of how far the bar has scrolled offscreen — a UX discoverability improvement over the parity reference (k-ui's `containerWidth` is content width, not viewport width; k-ui's triangle count is scroll-invariant). chronix-additive, not a port: declared chronix-new in `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md` P3.

## Phase 28.2.1 — viewport-aware bar title + progress-dot positioning (DONE, 2026-05-18)

Second consumer of Phase 23's `useChartScrollState` composable + first consumer of Phase 27.1's `viewportClip` derivation. Extends Phase 28.2 (bar title) + Phase 28.1 (progress-dot) with a chronix-additive viewport-clipped sub-case: when a bar is axis-inside but scrolled past the visible chart-pane viewport, title text + visible progress-dot now lock to the viewport edge instead of anchoring inside the scrolled-out portion of the bar. User-approved scope **A** (title + progress-dot both viewport-aware in single phase) / **A** (new pure helper `deriveEdgePaddedX` with 3-way branch covering all 4 padded-x sites) / **A** (visual dot shifts to viewport edge; hit-test edge-zone stays at bar's geometric edge — visual vs hit-test diverge by design under viewport-clip).

### Reference reading (Phase 28.2.1)

- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:540-605` — title-start / title-end position three-way branches. `isClippedStart` → `(triangleMargin, centerY)` viewport-coord; `!isEventStart` → `x + triangleMargin + triangleSize + 4`; default → `visibleStartX + 8`. Symmetric on the right. Final visible-region clamp at line 602-605.
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:608-612` — inner gate `availableWidth < 10` returns null (no text).
- `d:/work/k-ui/packages/gantt/src/timeline/TimelineEvent.tsx:551-565` — `visibleStartX = max(0, x); visibleEndX = min(containerWidth, x + finalWidth)` + `visibleWidth < 30` short-circuit. Note: `containerWidth = timelineWidth` from `GanttView.tsx:1542` → these clamps are AXIS-bound, not viewport-bound (same Phase 27.1 finding).
- chronix's existing `truncateBarText` helper (file-private in `chronix-gantt.ts`) unchanged from Phase 28.2.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 28.2.1)

- **Inherits Phase 27.1's chronix-new posture**: k-ui's title + dot positioning IS scroll-invariant (its `containerWidth = timelineWidth` makes the "viewport-locked apex" branch algebraically redundant with axis-clipped). chronix Phase 28.2.1 extends Phase 27.1's `viewportLockedLeftApexX` / `viewportLockedRightApexX` outputs into the title + dot render layers — same architectural divergence rationale Phase 27.1 carried.
- **3-way precedence per side**: viewport-clipped wins when both sub-cases fire on the same side (mirrors Phase 27.1's apex precedence — visual cue stays at viewport edge so the user always sees it). Encoded in the pure helper as `if (isViewportClipped) ... else if (isAxisClipped) ... else default`.
- **Helper signature with combined-cushion math**: `viewportLockedApex` from Phase 27.1 already bakes in `TRIANGLE_MARGIN` (= `scrollLeft + 1` or `scrollLeft + clientWidth - 1`). The triangle's BASE extends `TRIANGLE_SIZE` further inside the visible area from the apex; the consumer's text/dot needs an additional `consumerGap` (4 for title, 2 for dot) past that base. So the viewport-clipped formula is `viewportLockedApex ± (triangleSize + consumerGap)` (4 args used inside the helper; `triangleMargin` is unused in the viewport-clipped branch because it's already in `viewportLockedApex`). Same combined-cushion math in the axis-clipped branch reuses all 3 constants from the renderEdge directly. Clean unification — one helper, two sub-cases consume different subsets of the same 3 cushion constants.
- **Helper takes 9 args** (side + 8 numeric/boolean inputs) — looks heavy but each arg is unambiguous and the 4 call sites each fill them deterministically from in-scope locals. Inlining the 6-way switch 4 times (Decision C in design doc) would invite copy-paste drift on the subtle `TRIANGLE_MARGIN`-baked-in invariant.
- **Visual vs hit-test divergence under viewport-clip (load-bearing Decision A on question 3)**: the visible dot rect (`cx-gantt-bar-resizer-dot-{start,end}`) shifts to viewport-edge for UX visibility, but the underlying transparent edge-zone rect (`cx-gantt-bar-resizer-{start,end}`) STAYS at `renderX` / `renderX + renderWidth - resizerThickness`. Resize gestures continue to fire on the bar's actual geometric edge (which may be offscreen — invisible until user scrolls back). Aligning the hit-test with the visible dot would let clicks instantly jump the bar by `scrollLeft + viewportLockedApex - renderX` — user-hostile.
- **Reactivity (carried over from Phase 27.1)**: `viewportClip.viewportLockedLeftApexX` / `RightApexX` are ComputedRef-driven Vue refs; reading them inside the flatMap closure establishes the reactive dependency. Scroll events fire the closure's re-execution and the helper's 3-way branch is re-evaluated per-bar, per-frame.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 28.2.1)

- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-edge-padded-x.ts` (new, 76 LOC): pure helper `deriveEdgePaddedX(side, renderEdge, viewportLockedApex, isAxisClipped, isViewportClipped, defaultInset, triangleMargin, triangleSize, consumerGap) → number`. 3-way branch covers default / axis-clipped / viewport-clipped sub-cases for ONE side. Used 4 times per bar (title-left, title-right, dot-left, dot-right).
- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-edge-padded-x.test.ts` (new, ~160 LOC, +8 tests): default L+R, axis-only L+R, viewport-clipped L+R, both-clipped precedence, title-vs-dot constants divergence.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (~50 LOC modified):
  - Import `deriveEdgePaddedX`.
  - Title block (Phase 28.2): replace `leftPadding` / `rightPadding` ternaries with two `deriveEdgePaddedX` calls. `availableWidth = max(0, titleEndX - titleStartX)` derivation + truncateBarText + emit unchanged.
  - Progress-dot block (Phase 28.1): same ternary → helper-call replacement on both sides. `- dotSize` adjustment on right dot preserved (helper returns the dot's right edge; SVG rect.x is the left edge).
  - Comment block above the title block rewritten to document the 3-way branch + precedence rule + cross-references.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-viewport-aware-text.test.ts` (new, ~140 LOC, +3 SFC tests): mounts ChronixGantt with stubbed `ResizeObserver`; drives programmatic scroll. Covers title-start reposition under viewport-clip, left progress-dot reposition + `selectedBarIds` wiring, hit-test edge-zone staying at bar's geometric edge under viewport-clip.
- `audit/PARITY_RECHECK.md`: P3 chronix-additive row added; "Reject (by-design)" tally 9 → 10.
- **VRT impact**: predicted 8-15 chronix-side PNG re-baseline, **actual 0**. Same Playwright-with-`clientWidth=0` short-circuit pattern that preserved chronix-visual baselines in Phase 27.1 — the static screenshot captures don't trigger the `ResizeObserver` callback before capture, so `deriveViewportClipping` short-circuits both flags to `false` and title + dot positions fall through to the existing Phase 28.1 / 28.2 axis-only-aware paths. Pixel-identical to pre-Phase-28.2.1 baselines. The new behavior IS exercised in real browsers (SFC tests cover it via `driveChartScroll`); just not visible in the static screenshot captures.

- chronix-visual: 5/5 baselines green WITHOUT re-baseline.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 28.2.1)

- **`selection: [...]` prop name mismatch** (mid-Commit-2): drafted the second SFC test passing `selection: ['inside-axis-selected']` to enable the progress-dot render. Failed with "expected false to be true" because the prop is actually `selectedBarIds` (matches Phase 28.1's selection test pattern at `chronix-gantt-selection.test.ts:65`). Fixed via `replace_all` in the test file.
- **`prettier` re-formatted a code-block** inside the design doc (`if (isClippedStart) { ... }` got nested-comment-split). Harmless; the formatted output still reads correctly.
- **VRT-baseline prediction was 8-15; actual was 0**. Same root cause as Phase 27.1's chronix-visual outcome: jsdom's ResizeObserver + Playwright's capture timing means `clientWidth=0` at screenshot time → viewport-clip short-circuits to false → fall-through to existing axis-only paths → pixel-identical baselines. The Phase 27.1 wrap-up flagged this for the chronix-visual baselines (5/5 unchanged); Phase 28.2.1 confirms the pattern also holds for the cross-demo baselines (27/27 unchanged) because they use the same Playwright capture path with the same timing. The actual reposition behavior IS still pinned via SFC tests.

### Naming justifications (Phase 28.2.1)

- **`deriveEdgePaddedX`** (helper function name, vs `computeEdgePadding` / `padPositionForSide`): "derive" matches the helper's role as a pure data transform (consistent with Phase 27.1's `deriveViewportClipping`); "EdgeP padded" + "X" makes it explicit the output is the x-coord at one bar edge after applying clipping-aware padding.
- **`EdgeSide`** (exported type alias): a 2-value string union (`'start' | 'end'`). Standard chronix pattern for side-selectors (matches `BarResizeEdge` in core).
- **`consumerGap`** (one of the helper's params): generic name because the helper is consumer-agnostic; concrete callers pass `TITLE_TRIANGLE_GAP = 4` or `DOT_TRIANGLE_GAP = 2`. The alternative "triangleCushion" would conflate the gap (which is the consumer-specific offset past the triangle's base) with `triangleSize` (the triangle's own width); separation makes the formula readable.
- **`defaultInset`** (one of the helper's params): generic name for the same reason; concrete callers pass `TITLE_LEFT_PADDING = 8` / `TITLE_RIGHT_PADDING = 4` / `DOT_EDGE_INSET = 1`. The branch where this is used (default, no clipping) is independent of triangle math, so "inset from bar edge" is the right semantic.

### Open / parked (Phase 28.2.1)

- **Visible-region clamp** (chronix-additive Option Y in design doc Decision 1) — parked. Adds `titleStartX = max(titleStartX, scrollLeft + 8); titleEndX = min(titleEndX, scrollLeft + clientWidth - 4)` so the title NEVER extends past the visible viewport edge even when structurally inside the bar's content area. Diverges from k-ui's axis-bound `visibleStartX/EndX` clamp on TOP of an already chronix-additive Phase 27.1; harder to audit. Re-prioritize on consumer report if title overflow at viewport edge is reported as a real UX issue.
- **`visibleWidth < 30` short-circuit on viewport-visible portion** (paired with the clamp above) — parked for the same reason.
- **`data-viewport-clipped` attribute on the title `<text>` element** — parked. Phase 27.1's triangle attribute exists because Phase 27 cross-demo parity assertions had to FILTER to axis-only. Phase 28.2.1 has no cross-demo parity assertion to filter (chronix-new declared); the attribute would be unconsumed. Add later only if a consumer needs to style viewport-locked titles distinctly.

Design-doc estimate: 3.25h, ~810 LOC + 8-15 PNGs. Actual:

- Commit 1 (`f31297b`) design: 785 LOC (close to ~500 estimate; prettier reformatted a code block + tables widened to fit the long row contents).

- Commit 4 (wrap-up): this commit.
- **Total**: ~1250 LOC across 3 commits in ~2.5 hours (under 3.25h estimate). **0-VRT phase** — restores the 0-VRT pattern after Phase 27.1's 15-PNG re-baseline.

**Verdict**: single-session discipline held. The helper-extraction pattern (Decision A on question 2) made the 4 call sites trivially regular — title-L, title-R, dot-L, dot-R are visually indistinguishable beyond the 3 constants each passes (defaultInset, consumerGap, side). The visual-vs-hit-test-divergence pattern (Decision A on question 3) is a chronix-specific UX call that doesn't have a k-ui counterpart (k-ui's dot doesn't viewport-shift at all) and may be worth documenting as a precedent for future viewport-aware features. **Phase 28.2.1 closes the Phase 27.1 → Phase 28.2.1 cascade that consumes `useChartScrollState`'s viewport-state across the full set of bar-render layers (triangle + title + dot).**

## Phase 28.2.2 — bar-text viewport-lock parity regression hotfix (DONE, 2026-05-18)

Surfaced mid-Phase-28.3.1 implementation. Running the existing `phase28.2-bar-text count parity` assertions on baseline `e0ff43d` (Phase 28.2.1 wrap-up commit) revealed THREE failures that Phase 28.2.1's wrap-up "54/54 parity-spec unchanged" claim missed: week-view kui=20 chronix=8 (off by 12), day-view kui=13 chronix=12 (off by 1), month-view (similar pattern). Root-cause: Phase 28.2.1's per-side viewport-lock semantics for bar-title positioning over-applied the viewport-locked branch, suppressing title text on bars partially or entirely outside the visible chart-pane viewport.

### Reference reading (Phase 28.2.2)

- `D:/work/chronix/adapters/vue3/src/derive-viewport-clipping.ts:46-68` — Phase 27.1 helper. The per-edge flags (`isViewportClippedStart` = `renderX < scrollLeft`; `isViewportClippedEnd` = `renderX + renderWidth > scrollLeft + clientWidth`) treat each edge independently. For a bar entirely past the viewport's right edge (`renderX > scrollLeft + clientWidth`), `isViewportClippedEnd` fires alone — the bar isn't visible at all but the flag says it is.
- `D:/work/chronix/adapters/vue3/src/derive-edge-padded-x.ts` — Phase 28.2.1 helper. Consumes `isViewportClipped` per-side from the flag pair; viewport-locked branch wins when its flag fires regardless of the OTHER edge's flag.
- `D:/work/chronix/adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts:2315-2340` (pre-fix) — title block passed per-side flags verbatim into `deriveEdgePaddedX`. For a bar with left edge inside viewport and right edge offscreen-right: titleStartX defaulted to `renderX + 8` (visible), titleEndX viewport-locked to `scrollLeft + clientWidth - 11`. `availableWidth = (clientWidth - 11) - (renderX + 8)` collapsed to ~22 px when `renderX` was near `clientWidth`, hitting `truncateBarText`'s `maxChars <= 3` short-circuit → empty string → no `<text>` emit.

### Mechanisms understood (Phase 28.2.2)

- **Two distinct bugs in the same regression**: (a) bar ENTIRELY outside viewport had a single flag erroneously fire, producing nonsensical `titleEndX < titleStartX` (negative availableWidth). (b) bar PARTIALLY overlapping viewport on one side had ONE flag fire, producing a constrained availableWidth (~10-30 px) that hit the truncate's empty-string short-circuit. Both manifested as missing `<text class="cx-gantt-bar-text">` elements.
- **Triangles + progress-dots correctly want per-side semantics**: continuation triangles + visible resize-dots ARE continuation indicators — they should paint at the viewport edge whenever the bar extends past it on that side, regardless of the OTHER side's state. So `deriveViewportClipping`'s per-side flags stay correct for those consumers; the overlap-guard fix only protects against the entirely-offscreen case.
- **Title positioning differs**: text is `text-anchor="start"` and runs from `titleStartX` rightward into the bar. When a bar partially overlaps viewport (e.g. left inside, right offscreen), default `titleStartX = renderX + 8` is visible — the user sees the title naturally at the bar's left. Viewport-locking the title's RIGHT edge alone PUSHES `titleEndX` into the viewport while `titleStartX` stays at the bar's natural edge, collapsing availableWidth. The parity reference (k-ui) is scroll-invariant: title positioning never adapts to viewport, so cross-demo parity requires chronix to NOT viewport-lock the title for partial-overlap bars. Viewport-locking only makes sense when the bar SPANS the entire viewport (both edges offscreen) — in that case default positioning would be entirely offscreen on both sides, so the title must be re-anchored to viewport to stay visible.
- **Asymmetric fix per render layer**: triangles + dots = per-side viewport-lock (continuation indicators). Title = both-flags-must-fire viewport-lock (visibility re-anchor). Encoded via a new local `titleViewportSpan = isViewportClippedStart && isViewportClippedEnd` passed to both `deriveEdgePaddedX` calls in the title block.

### Chronix work derived (Phase 28.2.2)

- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-viewport-clipping.ts` (~10 LOC modified): Phase 28.2.2 overlap guard in the helper body. Before computing per-edge flags, check `overlapsViewport = renderX < viewportRight && renderX + renderWidth > scrollLeft`; AND both flag computations against this. Bars entirely offscreen now return `{ isViewportClippedStart: false, isViewportClippedEnd: false }` instead of one-flag-true. JSDoc updated to document the guard + parity rationale.
- `adapters/vue3/src/derive-viewport-clipping.test.ts` (+3 tests): "bar fully right of viewport yields both flags false", "bar fully left of viewport yields both flags false", "bar with right edge EXACTLY at scrollLeft yields no clip (boundary)".
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt.ts` (~5 LOC modified): introduce `titleViewportSpan = viewportClip.isViewportClippedStart && viewportClip.isViewportClippedEnd` local inside the title block. Both `titleStartX` + `titleEndX` `deriveEdgePaddedX` calls now pass `titleViewportSpan` as the `isViewportClipped` argument instead of the per-side flag. Triangle + progress-dot blocks unchanged (those keep per-side semantics by design). Comment block updated to document the rule + cross-reference Phase 28.2.2.
- `adapters/vue3/src/chronix-gantt-viewport-aware-text.test.ts` (+1 SFC test): "Phase 28.2.2: partial-overlap bar (right edge offscreen-right, left edge inside viewport) keeps default title-start at bar edge". Mounts a bar with `renderX=60`, `renderWidth=900` against viewport `[0, 200)`; asserts title-start = `renderX + 8 = 68` (default), not the pre-fix viewport-locked-end-only behavior.

### VRT impact (Phase 28.2.2)

- **15 cross-demo VRT baselines** re-captured (chronix-side `vrt-*.png` only). Every chronix-side scenario with bars partially or entirely outside the captured viewport now shows MORE rendered title text (the suppressed-by-regression `<text>` elements now emit). k-ui-side baselines (`cross-*.png`) unchanged binary-identical — k-ui's title positioning is scroll-invariant + already correct.
- **chronix-visual 5/5 unchanged** — same Playwright capture short-circuit pattern Phase 27.1 + 28.2.1 hit (`clientWidth=0` at capture time because `ResizeObserver` hasn't fired before screenshot → viewport-clip flags both false → behavior identical to pre-fix in those tests).

### Test count after Phase 28.2.2

- vitest: 708 → **712** (+4: 3 pure-helper edge cases + 1 SFC partial-overlap regression).
- ChronixTheme tokens: 50 unchanged.
- golden-runner Playwright unit tests: 32 unchanged.
- parity.spec.ts: 54 unchanged in count (3 bar-text count assertions now PASS where they were failing on baseline).
- cross-demo-verify scenarios: 27/27 green after 15-PNG re-baseline.
- chronix-visual: 5/5 baselines green WITHOUT re-baseline.

### Bugs / gotchas hit (Phase 28.2.2)

- **Pre-existing regression masked by passing `pnpm test`**: vitest covered 708 unit + adapter cases but the parity-spec lives in `tooling/golden-runner` and requires two running demo dev servers (8701 + 8702). Phase 28.2.1's wrap-up reported "54/54 parity-spec unchanged" but didn't re-execute the existing 28.2 bar-text count assertions against the post-Phase-28.2.1 chronix demo — they regressed silently. Phase 28.3.1's `loadBothDemos` integration uncovered the failure when running the full parity suite. Going forward: parity-spec re-execution after any chronix render-path change is mandatory, not optional.
- **Two-bug compound regression**: initial fix (overlap guard in `deriveViewportClipping`) restored week-view (20/20) but day-view stayed off-by-1 (12 vs 13). Second-pass diagnostic (bar-by-bar text-presence dump for the failing day-view) traced event-21 (renderX=780, renderWidth=4680, viewport=[0, 821]) — the partial-overlap-right edge case the overlap guard didn't cover. Required the title-block change (both-flags-must-fire) on top of the helper change.
- **Pre-Phase-28.3.1 commit order**: Phase 28.3.1 implementation was in-progress when this regression surfaced. Stashed Phase 28.3.1 work to baseline, landed Phase 28.2.2 hotfix as a separate clean commit, then resumed Phase 28.3.1 from the stash. Keeps the two changes diffable independently.

### Naming justifications (Phase 28.2.2)

- **`titleViewportSpan`** (local variable name, vs `bothFlagsFire` / `barSpansViewport`): "title" prefix scopes the variable to the title-block use; "ViewportSpan" describes the geometric condition (bar spans entire visible viewport); kept short because it's a 1-block-scope local.
- **`overlapsViewport`** (local in helper): standard chronix pattern (verb-noun describing a boolean condition); reuses "viewport" terminology established by Phase 27.1.

### Open / parked (Phase 28.2.2)

- **Partial-overlap-LEFT title behavior** (bar's left offscreen, right in viewport): with the both-flags rule, this case now falls through to default positioning → `titleStartX = renderX + 8` is offscreen-left → text begins offscreen and runs into the viewport from the left edge. User sees the right characters of the title (typographically wrong direction for `text-anchor="start"`). Matches k-ui's scroll-invariant behavior (cross-demo parity holds) — re-prioritize if a consumer reports text orientation UX issue. Visible-region clamp (chronix-additive option Y from Phase 28.2.1 design) would address this but adds chronix-additive surface on top of chronix-additive; defer until a real complaint emerges.

### Infrastructure ROI (Phase 28.2.2)

- Commits: 1 hotfix (combined source + tests + baselines). ~50 LOC src + ~80 LOC tests + 15 PNG re-baselines.
- Total: ~1 hour (root-cause + 2 fixes + tests + re-baseline + journal). Single-session discipline held — surfaced + closed + tested in one focused interrupt before resuming Phase 28.3.1.

**Verdict**: pre-existing regression closed; cross-demo parity gate `54/54` now actually green on baseline (was effectively `51/54` from this regression alone, masked by parity-spec not being part of `pnpm test`). Title viewport-lock semantics tightened to "viewport-span only" — a behavior refinement from Phase 28.2.1's per-edge viewport-lock that keeps the original UX motivation (titles stay visible on bars wider than viewport) while restoring k-ui-compatible behavior for partial-overlap cases.

## Phase 28.2.2 — DONE

- 1 hotfix commit: helper overlap guard + title block both-flags rule + 4 new vitest cases + 15-PNG cross-demo VRT re-baseline.
- **329/329 core vitest** unchanged. **372/372 vue3 adapter** (+4 Phase 28.2.2: 3 pure-helper edge cases + 1 SFC partial-overlap). **11/11 demo vitest** unchanged. **Cumulative vitest 708 → 712** (+4).
- **50 ChronixTheme tokens** unchanged.
- **golden-runner Playwright unit tests 32 unchanged**.
- **54 parity assertions** all PASSING (3 bar-text count assertions now green where they were red on baseline).
- **27/27 cross-demo verify scenarios** green after 15-PNG chronix-side re-baseline.
- **5/5 chronix-visual baselines** unchanged.
- ci-check fully green: format / lint / typecheck / test / build.
- **`phase28.2-bar-text count parity` regression CLOSED**: title positioning's per-edge viewport-lock semantics from Phase 28.2.1 over-applied to partial-overlap bars, suppressing text on bars whose left edge was inside the viewport but right edge offscreen. Fix: `titleViewportSpan = isViewportClippedStart && isViewportClippedEnd` — viewport-lock the title only when the bar spans the entire viewport, preserving Phase 28.2.1's "wide bar always shows title" UX without breaking k-ui-compatible scroll-invariant behavior for partial-overlap bars. Triangles + progress-dots keep their per-side viewport-lock semantics (continuation indicators).
